
-----title
九江（德化） (出生地)

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eb31d4fe46d342d89e1d6e00201d98aa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb31d4fe46d342d89e1d6e00201d98aa");'><span id='eb31d4fe46d342d89e1d6e00201d98aa_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1000&endYear=1000')">1000年</a>　冬，随父在京，父宋玘调任常州司理参军。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='591a1fab8d164a88becd28099e52b86c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("591a1fab8d164a88becd28099e52b86c");'><span id='591a1fab8d164a88becd28099e52b86c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>，22岁</div><div id='591a1fab8d164a88becd28099e52b86c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年6月29日</a>　六月二十九日，父宋玘卒于京城，力不克葬，权窆父柩于京郊。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='193e9d33da3c4827a4343d79c67fef91_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("193e9d33da3c4827a4343d79c67fef91");'><span id='193e9d33da3c4827a4343d79c67fef91_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1024')">1023-1024年</a>，28-29岁</div><div id='193e9d33da3c4827a4343d79c67fef91' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年10月</a>　十月，由开封府取解，乡试作《良玉不琢赋》，胥偃擢为第一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　冬，在京应举，始与晏殊交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年2月</a>　二月，在京应礼部试，作《采侯诗》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年2月</a>　二月，在京应礼部试，因作《德车结旌赋》失韵，被考落，文卷校勘官李宥袖其文卷见主考官刘筠，遂得中举。作品：德车结旌赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《元宪集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1155014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155014?labeling=true' target='_blank'>德车载旌赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155014")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155014'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155014'>君有至德，时乘大车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155014_comment'></div>当偃革以无外，乃结旌而有初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155014_comment'></div>奉驾陈仪，采物虽资于备设；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155014_comment'></div>鸣鸾示礼，旂旒匪俟于垂舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155014_comment'></div>顺考前经，铺闻往说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155014_comment'></div>谓戎事以既息，贵君车之有结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155014_comment'></div>雍容抚轼，盖藏饰以尚纯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155014_comment'></div>肃穆展铃，讵垂旓而就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155014_comment'></div>盖由抑乃盛饰，昭夫令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155014_comment'></div>虽冠品于舆服，蔑扬威于旆旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155014_comment'></div>肃轸无哗，方歛藏于斿厉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155014_comment'></div>驰轮有度，靡赫奕于緌缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155014_comment'></div>且夫礼有质文，器随用舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155014_comment'></div>车号乎德，则崇化于邦本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155014_comment'></div>旌结其表，则示仁于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155014_comment'></div>意自象见，名非人假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155014_comment'></div>君轩弭节，孰讶乎卷而怀之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155014_comment'></div>国乘制容，益显乎素为贵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155014_comment'></div>是知车之用兮，充德以成大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155014_comment'></div>旄之饰兮，辅威而孔昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155014_comment'></div>既武怒之不作，信军容而外销。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155014_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1155014", 1155014, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>组辔</span>启行，陋郊旌之孑孑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155014_comment'></div>错衡遵路，殊风旆之摇摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155014_comment'></div>若然则动有彝仪，文无异色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155014_comment'></div>虽严驾以备物，终去华而表德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155014_comment'></div>故使礼典攸重，民瞻不忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155014_comment'></div>皇皇整御，始中括于采章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155014_comment'></div>槛槛肃容，岂外扬于藻饰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155014_comment'></div>用能上载明德，旁昭缛仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155014_comment'></div>自驾言而戾止，殊幅裂以藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155014_comment'></div>升降惟寅，仅比非心之屋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155014_comment'></div>章明尽屏，宁同止猎之緌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155014_comment'></div>大矣哉，邦礼是崇，帝仪资始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155014_comment'></div>实务德以垂教，必收旌而昭理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155014_comment'></div>宜乎国容备而兵器销，率由兹而尽美。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1155014_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年3月18日</a>　三月十八日，于京师崇政殿受仁宗召对，与弟宋祁同榜进士及第，被擢为第一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年3月</a>　三月，在京，进士及第后有谢座主启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年4月7日</a>　四月七日，在京预琼林宴。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='00c138697620467c8fa9c36d70ce6ed2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("00c138697620467c8fa9c36d70ce6ed2");'><span id='00c138697620467c8fa9c36d70ce6ed2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>，29岁</div><div id='00c138697620467c8fa9c36d70ce6ed2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年8月</a>　八月，在京释褐为大理评事、襄州通判。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9cf303b4d24e49ebbf3a8bd860907315_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9cf303b4d24e49ebbf3a8bd860907315");'><span id='9cf303b4d24e49ebbf3a8bd860907315_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1036')">1026-1036年</a>，31-41岁</div><div id='9cf303b4d24e49ebbf3a8bd860907315' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　冬，被召还京，删定令文，有诗记事。作品：受诏论次令文逾月纲条未举。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_106432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>受诏论次令文踰月纲条未举</a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106432")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_106432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106432'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106432'>汉家甲令议蠲烦，曹札沈迷拥昼轩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106432'>城旦千条纷未举，始知黄老得名言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106432'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_106432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年7月12日</a>　七月十二日，在京试学士院，除太子中允，直史馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年11月</a>　十一月，在京为太子中允，参加圜丘大典，上《国阳大报颂》作品：国阳大报颂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1155579' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155579' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155579?labeling=true' target='_blank'>国阳大报颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155579")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155579'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155579'>臣闻职乎覆载，天地之化均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155579_comment'></div>推乎功德，祖宗之谊一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155579_comment'></div>化之均者其报等，故明察之祀，曾是而并升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155579_comment'></div>谊之一者其孝同，故妥侑之主，无嫌于交飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155579_comment'></div>此设教所以本神道，议礼所以沿人情者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155579_comment'></div>矧夫兆福畤于阳位，差谷旦于天正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155579_comment'></div>陟降惟寅，采物具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155579_comment'></div>三灵逆釐，四海来助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155579_comment'></div>对缛礼于盛际，进明德于升闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155579_comment'></div>遹骏有声，上帝穆其临汝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155579_comment'></div>敷闻于下，三后赫其在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155579_comment'></div>巍巍煌煌，礼之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155579_comment'></div>是则耿命之所集，至圣乃兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155579_comment'></div>精意之所禋，嘉生攸降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155579_comment'></div>著在耳目，合若符节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155579_comment'></div>天人之际，不其显哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155579_comment'></div>国家蓄五胜炎灵之精，圣上席四叶重雍之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155579_comment'></div>丕冒绵宇，休有神器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155579_comment'></div>若其冲用居质，渊泉而博厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155579_comment'></div>妙年纂服，神灵而敦敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155579_comment'></div>天光内发，乾亨首出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155579_comment'></div>金玉其度，神明其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155579_comment'></div>三年之谅闇，既言乃驩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155579_comment'></div>复旦之光华，重合于帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155579_comment'></div>建号之始，堲乎殄行，而朕师不震，有洸洸之武；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155579_comment'></div>持盈之际，秉具文德，而多士对越，有安安之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155579_comment'></div>奉养长乐，躬高世之三行，有匹夫之孝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155579_comment'></div>内睦公姓，亲在庭之五大，有家人之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155579_comment'></div>一夫未获，则矜而弗喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155579_comment'></div>一政未乂，必退而更化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155579_comment'></div>和气溢于万物，厚福浸于群氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155579_comment'></div>巩焉若泰山之加四维，昶焉如宏纲之经万目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155579_comment'></div>天下之大本举矣，帝者之丕功集矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155579_comment'></div>方且轸无灾之惧，愀若以荐辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155579_comment'></div>歌《小毖》之篇，周爰而求助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1155579_comment'></div>武铭遍于户席，汉谏缉乎帷囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1155579_comment'></div>谦尊而光，业久而大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1155579_comment'></div>天启渊虑，魄兆嘉贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1155579_comment'></div>若曰三服容于自损，而玉帛得以加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1155579_comment'></div>六膳可以自啬，而牲牷不敢爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1155579_comment'></div>况三年之祀，疏则怠焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1155579_comment'></div>七里之兆，往不劳止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1155579_comment'></div>幸天之相而岁之易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1155579_comment'></div>朕将再执笾豆，以郊见于神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1155579_comment'></div>令下于源，丝出而綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1155579_comment'></div>于是当国之辅，刺经之伦，峨峨以相趋，翼翼而旅议，莫不稽仙源之自，酌圣考之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1155579_comment'></div>谓夫皇基所开，系自真祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1155579_comment'></div>故先祠有景灵之谒，元命申锡，主乎魄宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1155579_comment'></div>故已事有玉清之拜，尊亲兼极，变于礼而得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1155579_comment'></div>先后不违，过乎恭而何害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1155579_comment'></div>定命兹允，前闻夐绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1155579_comment'></div>既而宝谷登实，良农告休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1155579_comment'></div>日舍于箕，卦御乎坎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1155579_comment'></div>嶰窍律裁，同一气而未融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1155579_comment'></div>汉蕝栖野，缮多仪而豫定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1155579_comment'></div>于时百工庀具，千官联职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1155579_comment'></div>上公端委，誓于文昌之坐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1155579_comment'></div>天子淳濯，斋于端闱之寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1155579_comment'></div>屏舜膻而易馈，掩汉笥而停谳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1155579_comment'></div>澡雪天虑，秋游气辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1155579_comment'></div>俄而纷藻仗，出皇居，烦真场，跻太室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1155579_comment'></div>祝嘏并诏，臣工胥集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1155579_comment'></div>贵声之乐，登歌于堂上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1155579_comment'></div>合食之主，流出于户外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1155579_comment'></div>俯伏奠献，悽怆斋明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1155579_comment'></div>迪神贶而漙将，励孝思而极挚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1155579_comment'></div>始复御威辂，翳华芝，纤阿扶轮，大丙前马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1155579_comment'></div>抑繁吹而不作，溯阳郊而徐骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1155579_comment'></div>军辎雷动，神旂电舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1155579_comment'></div>八鸾异响而均和，六龙骈首而如舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1155579_comment'></div>豪英之士，玉色而同舆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1155579_comment'></div>葩华之云，金柯而拥盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1155579_comment'></div>豹尾树后，皆为省中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1155579_comment'></div>钩陈旁翊，是严帝座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1155579_comment'></div>背天阙，轹都门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1155579_comment'></div>三条荷衢而平趣帷宫，百灵护野而遂至祠所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1155579_comment'></div>皇羽设邸，熉幄缀珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1155579_comment'></div>门䆗窱而表旌，天穹崇而垂幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1155579_comment'></div>若夫圆坛中立，神垓递降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1155579_comment'></div>缀食惟旅，陪祀相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1155579_comment'></div>夷酋司燎，田首施烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1155579_comment'></div>且其罍云房俎，羽林秀华之品，宿设而芬树；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1155579_comment'></div>凫钟凤箾，琴絙瑟越之器，凝锵而声展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1155579_comment'></div>龙常琼钑，飞軨疏毂之乘，夹右乎道周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1155579_comment'></div>星枪𨌥弩，戴鹖被绣之师，髬髵于壝次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1155579_comment'></div>日在癸丑夜半冬至，百执就列，九宾相仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1155579_comment'></div>不敖不吴，有严有翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1155579_comment'></div>皇帝被天兖，执镇圭，俨邃旒，郤黄屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1155579_comment'></div>槃匜奉濯，亲就于东罍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1155579_comment'></div>茨夏摐音，徐升于午陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1155579_comment'></div>上帝富媪，南向异席，尊之至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1155579_comment'></div>烈祖神宗，左方并侑，情之尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1155579_comment'></div>天子一献以致虔，藩戚参奠而成礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1155579_comment'></div>粉庶豆以孔硕，扬信辞而无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1155579_comment'></div>歌钟咏德，蔼坑谷而皆盈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1155579_comment'></div>羽籥振容，率鸟兽而咸舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1155579_comment'></div>连珠合璧，属于象者无不歆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1155579_comment'></div>乔岳翕河，统乎神者无不秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1155579_comment'></div>群官分命以惟恪，众神受职而交驩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1155579_comment'></div>酌福饮以浮椒，峙槱薪而炽燎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1155579_comment'></div>皇猷允塞，熙事备成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1155579_comment'></div>回雕舆，御帐殿，冠剑旅贺，兵师齐跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1155579_comment'></div>逮长日之升晷，麾洪颐而复路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1155579_comment'></div>岧峣南阙，国贮天临之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1155579_comment'></div>肤寸东云，民希雨施之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1155579_comment'></div>既而端凤扆，揭鸡竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1155579_comment'></div>大令辰告，而在邦必闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1155579_comment'></div>众眚并肆，而与民更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1155579_comment'></div>是日也，涂歌邑颂，仁翔德洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1155579_comment'></div>逮鳏已责，优繇缓调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1155579_comment'></div>在疵者濯，居幽者炤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1155579_comment'></div>尽解犯命之网，措刑于三千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1155579_comment'></div>无出今年之租，兴颂于什一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1155579_comment'></div>亦既让德不处，归勋有恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1155579_comment'></div>练吉日，朝密都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1155579_comment'></div>叙拜贶之仪，罄谢成之悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1155579_comment'></div>再荷百禄，以绥兆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1155579_comment'></div>盛节能事，斯为至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1155579_comment'></div>臣尝学旧史，窃订大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1155579_comment'></div>以为宋虽旧邦，而其德维新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1155579_comment'></div>郊虽典祀，而厥应尤显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1155579_comment'></div>当盛礼之草具也，两宫叶议，周旋抑畏，固避号荣之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1155579_comment'></div>上仪之将展也，九河顺道，切和疏写，亟舒昏割之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1155579_comment'></div>吉土之亲飨也，隆冬变候，密清和照，讫无阴霾之祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1155579_comment'></div>是三烈者，不待瞽史而识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1155579_comment'></div>天意之悦，无烦巧历而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1155579_comment'></div>帝运之隆，砰隐乎殊休，觉悟乎黎献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1155579_comment'></div>跨风邃古，垂照来今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1155579_comment'></div>将使允烁者咀其馀甘，猗那者照其绝焰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1155579_comment'></div>斟酌饱满，饬厥性而用和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1155579_comment'></div>滋液渗漉，泳湛恩而无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1155579_comment'></div>非我休运，其畴宜之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1155579_comment'></div>而臣污韨朝伦，滥巾册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1155579_comment'></div>陪委粟之毖祀，叨甘泉之奉引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1155579_comment'></div>目饱懿铄，心萌咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1155579_comment'></div>罢黼绣之张，获闻于夜诵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1155579_comment'></div>均蟋蟀之候，难默于秋唫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1155579_comment'></div>愿纾感发之诚，少抃鸿钧之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1155579_comment'></div>拜手流汗，谨次颂云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_138_1155579'>上帝屹坛兮崇造天，二圣侑享兮严吉蠲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1155579_comment'></div>神光焜上兮风肃然，钦柴皇燎兮升高烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1155579_comment'></div>肃斯露泽兮浸群元，叶风顺气兮翱天渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1155579_comment'></div>垠开阃决兮曼寿延，表世题期兮弥亿年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_141_1155579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年11月</a>　十一月，在京为太子中允，作《进国阳大报颂表》作品：进国阳大报颂表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进国阳大报颂表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155526")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155526'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155526'>臣伏以日在太初之历，是谓履长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155526_comment'></div>天随帝者之居，兹焉临飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155526_comment'></div>扢三垓而昭事，坐两观以均禧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155526_comment'></div>遍朝真驭之下都，翕受群元之厚福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155526_comment'></div>含生鼓舞，协气陶烝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155526_comment'></div>忝蹈德以泳仁，宜交中而发外<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155526_comment'></div>窃念臣单门下品，弱植浅中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155526_comment'></div>被至化之纯深，副大猷之馀绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155526_comment'></div>翘然在沚，厕君子之育材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155526_comment'></div>间或登高，乏大夫之能赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155526_comment'></div>属承平之嗣旦，讲容典以和神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155526_comment'></div>南北异正而并修，祖宗以侑而交献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155526_comment'></div>周游六气，乘之而健行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155526_comment'></div>肸蚃万灵，屑然而著感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155526_comment'></div>目美光之若昼，钦众瑞以如山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155526_comment'></div>矧当清道之辰，已预皇轩之引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155526_comment'></div>瞻威咫尺，禀训蟺蜎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155526_comment'></div>庆千载以亲逢，畅四支而内抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155526_comment'></div>幸联儒馆，难默颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155526_comment'></div>惭积日以庀词，邈谈天而几殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155526_comment'></div>仅成累句，式赞盛容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155526_comment'></div>均子夏之一词，曷□邦体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155526_comment'></div>本虞初之小说，敢预家流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155526_comment'></div>仰渎程观，弥增震愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155526_comment'></div>谨夙夜斋祓，撰成《国阳大报颂》一篇，随表上进以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155526_comment'></div>干浼宸扆，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1155526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155526'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155526_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　春，在京为太子中允，有诗挽张知白。作品：赠太傅中书令张文节公挽词三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠太傅中书令张文节公挽词三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106977")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106977'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106977'>素范流邦册，昌言溢帝聪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106977'>三台应天老，万事问胡公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106977'>道有如弦直，生嗟委蜕穷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106977'>令君兼上傅，衮敛贲遗忠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106977'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106977_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106976?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106976'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106976'>昔命光三事，今嗟赎百身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106976'>堂无织蒲妾，车有吐茵人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106976'>台坼层氛夜，槐凋故府春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106976'>空馀相国第，不与势家邻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106976_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106976'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106976_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106975?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106975'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106975'>平日开黄阁，兹辰奠素旗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106975'>留侯尝辟谷，岩说遂骑箕。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106975'>天迥哀笳咽，林长导翣迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106975'>行人此堕泪，何必岘亭碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106975_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106975'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106975_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　本年，在京为太子中允，于刘筠宅结识僧智成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　约于本年，在京为太子中允，受命祠东太一宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　约于本年，在京为太子中允，有诗寄杨寺丞。作品：杨寺丞以新集见授。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_106671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨寺丞以新集见授<span class='inlineComment2'>（君与仆尝于荆州聚学）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1028年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106671")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106671'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106671'>荆台杯酒接慇勤，已是缇灰十五春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106671'>学舍早欣游雾露，辞条今服际天人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106671'>沈居雌蜺那知赏，叶牖神龙更骇真。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106671'>侍上可能无狗监，子虚赋就长卿贫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106671'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106671_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　约于本年，在京为太子中允，与范镇定交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年1月26日</a>　正月二十六日，在京为太子中允，有诗述怀。作品：己巳孟春二十六日作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_106547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己巳孟春二十六日作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年1月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106547")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106547'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106547'>纠缠空惊祸福频，沈舟未拯更摧轮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106547'>山头枉是轻廷尉，天上何容著蹇人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106547'>南国祭牺堪畏楚，东门猎犬尚尤秦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106547'>当涂莫竦支离诮，坐受朝家十束薪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106547'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　春，在京为太子中允，与李淑同饯刘筠赴知庐州任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年5月11日</a>　五月十一日，在京为太子中允，因《天圣令》书成，获赐勋一转，有诗谢吕夷简、夏竦。作品：受诏同编修敕令终篇例赐勋一转谢参与东平会稽二公。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_106679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>受诏同编修敕令终篇例赐勋一转谢参预东平会稽二公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年5月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106679")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106679'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106679'>法家高议集朝緌，成绩连茅被帝晖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106679'>均赏已知羊胃烂，铭恩偏觉鼠肝微。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106679'>泥涂枉入鸿钧用，腹背还凭逸翮飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106679'>天禄半生瘨眩病，犹堪持帚扫朱扉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106679'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106679_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年8月11日</a>　八月十一日，在京为太子中允，受命考试开封府举人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年11月9日</a>　十一月九日，在京为太子中允，观皇太后刘氏上寿礼，作长诗记之。作品：冬至观两宫盛礼奏御。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_107083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬至观两宫盛礼奏御</a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年11月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107083")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_107083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107083'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107083'>帝运姚华协，天元汉历长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107083'>三正来复旦，万寿此称觞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107083'>洛宅均中景，涂山采旧章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107083'>礼文穷竹素，欢意动梯航。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107083'>稷野茅联位，轩筠縠向阳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107083'>中天倚华阙，大火敞明堂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107083'>交铩髬髵队，填街隐辚装。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107083'>九关凝协气，复道伫清光。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107083'>子事蒸蒸极，宸仪穆穆扬。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107083'>母慈尊莫二，君拜祉无疆。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107083'>饰喜仙园奏，薰空佛土香。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107083'>含饴先侑宴，袭衮始宾王。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107083'>䆗窱宫门狄，谁何陛楯郎。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_107083'>长绅纷拱著，珍佩蔼森璋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_107083'>树次天开帟，储恩斗具浆。<div id='poem_sentence_14_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_107083'>风乌迎细转，霞燎俨相望。<div id='poem_sentence_15_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_107083'>辨御辰承盖，呼鞭辇出房。<div id='poem_sentence_16_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_107083'>云咸薄金石，星日上旂常。<div id='poem_sentence_17_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_107083'>逸缀朱干动，多仪的马骧。<div id='poem_sentence_18_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_107083'>麟题公有姓，鹭羽客分行。<div id='poem_sentence_19_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_107083'>上宰陈瑶爵，黎贤抃绣裳。<div id='poem_sentence_20_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_107083'>祈龄后天老，介福委山穰。<div id='poem_sentence_21_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_107083'>翼翼心同竭，渠渠泽载霶。<div id='poem_sentence_22_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_107083'>诗弦满坑谷，庖味益圆方。<div id='poem_sentence_23_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_107083'>盛掩钧台旧，仪高鲁观祥。<div id='poem_sentence_24_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_107083'>深仁跂喙逮，嘉唱股肱良。<div id='poem_sentence_25_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_107083'>茨夏随天步，鱼龙屏戏场。<div id='poem_sentence_26_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_107083'>晏温澄象纬，渗漉暨要荒。<div id='poem_sentence_27_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_107083'>瑞典精销祲，涂歌圣择狂。<div id='poem_sentence_28_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_107083'>樵苏无发哂，崖略蹈皇纲。<div id='poem_sentence_29_107083_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_107083'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_107083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年12月29日</a>　除夜，在京为太子中允，有诗述怀。作品：己巳岁除夜有感。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_107077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己巳岁除夜有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107077")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_107077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107077'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107077'>明晦互推斥，中都芳岁阑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107077'>星回迫旧次，籥暖送馀寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107077'>来辰茧有绪，去境环无端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107077'>天运故相易，人心那独安。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107077'>怀此不能寐，揽衣强盘桓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107077'>疏恐缓馀带，危惕整尘冠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107077'>耿耿烛焰直，凄凄霜气酸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107077'>城头陨高木，庭下败丛兰。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107077'>抚臆累新欷，掩觞沈故欢。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107077'>况乃蹈世网，虚名争控抟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107077'>挟册滥书府，振缨玷王官。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107077'>东序罗圭瑞，西雍集鹓鸾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107077'>昏瞳眩宝肆，短翼厕仙翰。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_107077'>纵尔值藏疾，何容久素餐。<div id='poem_sentence_13_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_107077'>泛泛骚客凫，坎坎诗人檀。<div id='poem_sentence_14_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_107077'>宁无要路津，所畏在蹒跚。<div id='poem_sentence_15_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_107077'>枳棘附骥尾，纬萧戏龙蟠。<div id='poem_sentence_16_107077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_107077_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年3月</a>　三月，在京为太子中允，观新进士琼林宴，有诗记事。作品：庚午春观新进士锡宴琼林苑因书所见。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_107124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午春观新进士锡宴琼林苑因书所见</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107124")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_107124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107124'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107124'>秘苑仪星地，群英得隽年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107124'>飞緌鲸浦右，供帐斗城偏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107124'>表道槐阴直，凌氛柞影圆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107124'>丛楹开玉宇，华组会琼筵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107124'>湛湛融君渥，渠渠奖士贤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107124'>银珰尊右席<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：中贵人主宴。）</span>，绿帻佐双笾<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：太官先置。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107124'>饰喜优坊伎，均恩醵礼钱<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107124'>沼浮渑酒渌，坻聚舜庖膻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107124'>场迥歌声合，风回舞节妍。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107124'>柳疑添绀幄，鹦解啄鸣弦。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107124'>臣藿心倾日，需云象在天。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107124'>绨囊赍睿什<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：中席，使者以御诗驰赐。）</span>，钿轴照儒篇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107124'>宝思垂霓烂，欢声抃岳传。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_107124'>珍台纷蹇产，翠气浩宛延<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_107124'>池讶阳乌浴，桥疑汉鹊填。<div id='poem_sentence_14_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_107124'>千夫拔河索，三令夺标船。<div id='poem_sentence_15_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_107124'>帐殿沧波匝，钩梯复道连。<div id='poem_sentence_16_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_107124'>瑶甍轩凤羽，云岛压鳌颠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_107124'>牺觡驯灵囿，天麰蔽大田。<div id='poem_sentence_18_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_107124'>江头拔兰紫，林下摘樱鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_19_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_107124'>玉藻初盈沼，神芝欲冒廛。<div id='poem_sentence_20_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_107124'>阳沟连禹洫，阴石骇秦鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_21_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_107124'>冰静恩鱼出，园空瑞鹄旋。<div id='poem_sentence_22_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_107124'>缭垣包井落，别渚上风烟。<div id='poem_sentence_23_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_107124'>金埒争镳地，珠翳射雉阡。<div id='poem_sentence_24_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_107124'>去辎雷远陌，归袂藻平川。<div id='poem_sentence_25_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_107124'>乍集储胥外，还经馺娑前。<div id='poem_sentence_26_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_107124'>子云嗟寂寞，无思状甘泉。<div id='poem_sentence_27_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_107124'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_107124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_107124'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_107124_0'>⑴ 自注：诸君子合钱以劳供帐优伶之费。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_107124_0'>⑵ 自注：复镂印《大学》《儒行》二篇以赐。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_13_107124_0'>⑶ 自注：此以下并述苑中池上景物之盛。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_107124_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　冬，继母朱夫人卒，退居畿邑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　冬，在京为继母守丧，安陆守舍儿馈丹橘一箧，感而作诗。作品：天禧初侨寓安陆，有宅一区，尝于斋前手植橘树才尺余许。未几擢第，随牒游方。天圣庚午冬屏居畿邑，守舍儿自安陆馈余丹橘一箧，因曰此即斋前所植。抚物怀旧，凄然不平者久之。因成感咏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_107079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天禧初侨寓安陆有宅一区尝于斋前手植橘树才尺馀许未几擢第随牒游方天圣庚午冬屏居畿邑守舍儿自安陆馈余丹橘一箧因曰此即斋前所植抚物怀旧悽然不平者久之因成感咏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107079")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_107079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107079'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107079'>昔年封檗栽，生意颇柔脆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107079'>今兹见丹实，落落如星丽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107079'>斯果号难成，常踰豫章岁<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：此木不十年不实。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107079'>孤根何为者，尚记吾庐地。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107079'>蔽芾讵因棠，连蜷乃同桂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107079'>厥包千里遥，守舍重缇惠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107079'>金颗照病眸，霜津益痟肺。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107079'>却算去里年，十听秋鸿唳。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107079'>无复陆绩怀，宁图李衡计。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107079'>他时攀树悲，讵减金城涕。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107079'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_107079_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　冬，在京为继母守丧，作序送僧智成。作品：送成上人序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1155567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送成上人序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155567")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155567'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155567'>天圣戊辰岁，余尝过候故内阁中山公，姑与公门友成上人者交臂于席间，微言软音，时落耳界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155567_comment'></div>自是数与之会，而亟饮其和，且慕其畸于人，而不与人异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155567_comment'></div>既而中山出守淝上，师振锡而从之，蔼然风期，深入法乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155567_comment'></div>一室金粟，有施饭之缘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155567_comment'></div>四海彦威，领弥天之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155567_comment'></div>胜集未几，宗工云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155567_comment'></div>孤云匪心，飞鸟随翼，背淮千里，聿来上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155567_comment'></div>庚午冬，余茹忧去官，屏处寰内，思文惠然策足，顾我于幽忧之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155567_comment'></div>悲心所熏，病膜如刮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155567_comment'></div>老龙死矣，空成奓户之惊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155567_comment'></div>泰山颓乎，弥感负墙之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155567_comment'></div>敛容申悼，徘徊久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155567_comment'></div>示视世缘，益足多者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155567_comment'></div>一日踵门告别，且求赠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155567_comment'></div>余曰：「儒家者流，道诗书，服人伦足矣，安识夫方之外耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155567_comment'></div>而又京师苾刍，方以俗谛罪我，将焉用之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155567_comment'></div>师曰：「不也，尘劳之与道爱，其缚均焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155567_comment'></div>今夫诵贯花之书，服界稻之衣，崇布金之刹，是种种者，于我法乃捕鱼取兔具耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155567_comment'></div>茍泥于此，虽吾师犹阿焉，彼求封之仁者何害？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155567_comment'></div>今将相造乎忘言之地，乃以言为病耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155567_comment'></div>余感其勤，因叙其所以而为之赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1155567_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　冬，有诗寄李淑，哭刘筠。作品：前岁春，仆与献臣同饯常山公于苑西。曾未再期，已均师门之痛。兼承即日亲奉攒涂，追往悼今，哽涕无已。因成短诗抒感，谅心契之同戚也。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106751' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106751' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106751?labeling=true' target='_blank'>前岁春仆与献臣同饯常山公于苑西曾未再期已均师门之痛兼承即日亲奉攒涂追往悼今哽涕无已因成短诗抒感谅心契之同戚也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106751")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106751_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106751'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106751'>昔岁西郊饯，曾瞻出守麾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106751'>今年东第哭，便叹哲人萎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106751'>辰巳空成谶，膏肓不遇医。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106751'>诘朝闻衮敛，心折寝门悲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106751_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106751'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106751_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　本年，丁忧前，在京判登闻鼓院，为三司户部判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年3月</a>　三月，在京为继母守丧，王硕出知潭州，作诗送之。作品：余卧病畿邑，御史王君假守潭楚，道出于舍下，特见存访，且寻先子之旧，钦承风仪，因为诗抒感云。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_107104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>余卧病畿邑御史王君假守潭楚道出于舍下特见存访且寻先子之旧钦承风仪因为诗抒感云</a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107104")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_107104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107104'>病客卧穷里，衡扉掩残春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107104'>隳官道家藏，窜迹农廛民。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107104'>朝罗噪饥雀，暮席流芳尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107104'>尸居恍踰岁，踵息动弥旬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107104'>忽讶绛鞲隶，传呼越郊畛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107104'>蹀躞千馀骑，雍容两朱轮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107104'>言是楚邦守，来过安邑贫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107104'>固宜辨贵弃，乃尔存艰辛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107104'>此道古为重，馀风今已沦。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107104'>物色认平素，载言接慇勤。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107104'>始悟先子旧，早笃尝僚亲。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107104'>孤心极摧橹，感涕浩盈巾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107104'>追念舞勺岁，已识栖鸾人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_107104'>师筵奉函席，学舍操书筠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_107104'>童牙自忘丑，诗钵或娱宾。<div id='poem_sentence_14_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_107104'>公时摛句赏，谓是天麒麟。<div id='poem_sentence_15_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_107104'>亲擘彩笺赠，勉我期日新<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：君尝作诗贶余，多所奖勖。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_107104'>汝南丏题品，有道定人伦。<div id='poem_sentence_17_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_107104'>自尔一暌剌，中年婴世纷。<div id='poem_sentence_18_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_107104'>天圣绍休绪，顿网横无垠。<div id='poem_sentence_19_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_107104'>鸾鹄不藏翼，虬蜗无遁鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_20_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_107104'>余时滥隗始，骧首摩苍旻。<div id='poem_sentence_21_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_107104'>司徒揖元叔，天子第平津。<div id='poem_sentence_22_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_107104'>甲科廷尉属，再命宫坊臣。<div id='poem_sentence_23_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_107104'>黄香入东观，贾谊过西秦。<div id='poem_sentence_24_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_107104'>䌷绎金匮室，珥彤瑶水滨。<div id='poem_sentence_25_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_107104'>登瀛识褚马，颂汉希渊云。<div id='poem_sentence_26_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_107104'>一朝泣风树，九死存馀焄。<div id='poem_sentence_27_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_107104'>中都索米后，老圃种瓜辰。<div id='poem_sentence_28_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_107104'>惠然下车揖，高义倾前闻。<div id='poem_sentence_29_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_107104'>却计髧髦日，二纪如逡巡。<div id='poem_sentence_30_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_107104'>今形虽隐几，昔训尚铭绅。<div id='poem_sentence_31_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_107104'>丈人笃求旧，偷俗将还淳。<div id='poem_sentence_32_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_107104'>湘水澹苍野，衡峰凌紫氛。<div id='poem_sentence_33_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_107104'>泽节首南夏，瑶魁瞻邃宸。<div id='poem_sentence_34_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_107104'>恋阙魏公子，吊贤楚灵均。<div id='poem_sentence_35_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_107104'>公怀佐时略，宜树光朝勋。<div id='poem_sentence_36_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_107104'>奚为远问俗，惜此徒伤神。<div id='poem_sentence_37_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_107104'>宣室懋清问，华光钦宝邻。<div id='poem_sentence_38_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_107104'>行行爱玉体，趋节伫来臻。<div id='poem_sentence_39_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_107104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_107104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_107104'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_107104_0'>⑴ 自注：景德中，余侍先子为弋阳督邮，君时勾稽属邑，始授余以学术。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_107104_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　约于本年，在京为继母守丧，作《感鸡赋》作品：感鸡赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《元宪集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1155013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感鸡赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155013")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155013'>予寓居畿邑，有里中男子蒋福者多畜群鸡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155013_comment'></div>内一鸡三足，其一足拳而弗用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155013_comment'></div>一鸡独足，能饮啄嬉戏，与群鸡上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155013_comment'></div>噫，祥眚之事，予不得而推，但感其物理之异而为赋云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1155013'>伊元化之无私兮，播群形以平施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155013_comment'></div>纷肖象而寓质，若巧钧之制器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155013_comment'></div>鳞者俾夫沉泳兮，角弗施于猛鸷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155013_comment'></div>引羽族而普观兮，足惟两而已备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155013_comment'></div>茍损益于天分兮，匪生生之本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155013_comment'></div>何此匹鸡，理绝常区？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155013_comment'></div>或踸踔而独止，或疣赘而联趺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155013_comment'></div>并鸣翔于桀次，亦饮啄乎庭隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155013_comment'></div>徒观其一，则缀不用之爪，剩无名之肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155013_comment'></div>象非同于海鳖，名有忝于阳乌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155013_comment'></div>其一则践孤立之危，靡全形之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155013_comment'></div>追山夔以同号，希商羊而并翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155013_comment'></div>宁真宰之好异兮，伊微禽之我惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155013_comment'></div>感天分之有常，循生涯而各得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155013_comment'></div>不决拇而龁枝，讵日黔而浴白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155013_comment'></div>蚿百足而蛇怜，蚓无心而土食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155013_comment'></div>将减此而益彼，惧速尤而长慝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155013_comment'></div>姑美恶之两忘兮，庶元和之来宅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1155013_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年1月1日</a>　正月一日，在京为继母守丧，有诗述怀。作品：京师故僚以余退居近畿数赐存问因叙怀自感。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年12月</a>　十二月，在京服除，迁太常丞，判户部勾院，同修起居注。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年12月</a>　十二月，忧阙还台，有诗寄李淑、郑戬。作品：忧阙诣台先寄献臣天休二学士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_106666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忧阕诣台先寄献臣天休二学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106666")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106666'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106666'>去国三年恨，还台九死馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106666'>凄凉曾釜粟，感咽晏楹书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106666'>鲋勺怀穷辙，鸡栖整故车。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106666'>惟当亲益友，叙阔费涟如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106666'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年12月24日</a>　十二月二十四日，在京为左正言，坐谏废郭皇后事，被罚铜二十斤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　本年，在京判户部勾院，上劄子论三事。作品：论蠲除杂税劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_1155547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论蠲除杂税劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155547")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155547'>臣草茅之姿，光华遘运，近承人乏，入倅计司，惟厥吏员，实掌民版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155547_comment'></div>以一介驽缓之质，阅四海征赋之益，徒尔首公，无以纾责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155547_comment'></div>辄怀管穴，思报毫分，罔避严诛，仰干睿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155547_comment'></div>臣闻立简易之法，则民不惑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155547_comment'></div>去因缘之奸，则吏无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155547_comment'></div>省簿领则要可举，一赋税则取有名，此皆治道之所繇，而历世之无改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155547_comment'></div>臣窃见当今正税之外，杂赋至繁，诡制异科，丑名暴歛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155547_comment'></div>原其所自，由来甚迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155547_comment'></div>盖自唐室解纽，五朝挺灾，孱王僭侯，盗据方国，坏合彻之典，取一切之宜，掊尅无厌，禁令自出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155547_comment'></div>于是有身丁地头之赋，农具牛皮之征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155547_comment'></div>鬻酒则户出曲钱，煮海则家增盐价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155547_comment'></div>虽与民更始，而弊制尚存，官司因循，惮于改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155547_comment'></div>故使尧舜之代，无桀貉之中，虽臣之愚，窃以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155547_comment'></div>今纵不能荡涤横赋，以宽民财；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155547_comment'></div>犹当釐易旧名，少近王道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155547_comment'></div>臣愚以谓可取杂名税钱及派纳之色，不移旧数，合为一号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155547_comment'></div>削去季世剥害之品，作为我朝较画之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155547_comment'></div>示之于民，则耳目易晓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155547_comment'></div>委之于吏，则条贯难欺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155547_comment'></div>录于官曹，则文籍不烦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155547_comment'></div>供乎财用，则称谓差美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155547_comment'></div>此旧入无秋毫之损，新规有指掌之易，丕变讹谬，垂于经常，实天下之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155547_comment'></div>如允臣所见，乞下三司，令子细勘会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155547_comment'></div>见今天下诸杂税钱外沿钱名目贯百闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155547_comment'></div>然后取其实数，合为一号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155547_comment'></div>逐年折变，自从旧法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155547_comment'></div>斯皆防患制法，遭时垂统者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155547_comment'></div>臣伏见国朝以来诏数下，而建条比牒连名，充曹牣府，烦科碎目，与日而滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155547_comment'></div>每罚一罪，断一事，有司引用，皆连篇累牍，不能遍举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155547_comment'></div>率不数岁，则别加论次，谓之编敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155547_comment'></div>盖欲条贯饬尽，纲目毕张，大可含元，细不容发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155547_comment'></div>而抵冒未绝，风流寖滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155547_comment'></div>一令之下，则奸生令表；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155547_comment'></div>一禁之设，则罪出禁先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155547_comment'></div>示于人则若教猱，施于事则如紊纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1155547_comment'></div>此皆不循其本，而求之于末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1155547_comment'></div>将欲措刑辟，跻仁寿者，不亦难乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1155547_comment'></div>夫恢恢有条，重而必罚者，本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1155547_comment'></div>事事曲制，轻而易犯者，末也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1155547_comment'></div>本不举则巨猾徼倖，末专任则细民罹灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1155547_comment'></div>今之诏条，病在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1155547_comment'></div>陛下幸加大惠，惜皇猷之未畅，深诏执事，精覈旧文，欲因盛时，遂定丕律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1155547_comment'></div>臣以谓不一劳者不永逸，无远虑者必近忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1155547_comment'></div>今虽定之，后必复改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1155547_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1155547_comment'></div>制度不立，贤愚杂议故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1155547_comment'></div>为之计者，莫若尽取改行诏敕与律文相校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1155547_comment'></div>律有本条而敕意小异者，则改而入律；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1155547_comment'></div>律无本条而名项别立者，则编而为敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1155547_comment'></div>况唐律之内，废条已多，若擿去旧文，益作新例，亦前王损益之常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1155547_comment'></div>人情不能无过，王道禁乎太察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1155547_comment'></div>其约束之烦语，官司之小禁，宜一切荡除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1155547_comment'></div>盖去之不足害治体，存之徒以饰罪梯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1155547_comment'></div>法轻不能绳奸豪，文密足以污良善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1155547_comment'></div>臣又闻王者之制，揭若日月，动如雷霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1155547_comment'></div>其言易而文，其禁切而广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1155547_comment'></div>伏见今之编敕者，繁长猥俗，与府县文移无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1155547_comment'></div>用字乖舛，异辞重复，宁所谓明白温醇之旨耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1155547_comment'></div>实由不专任达识大儒，而多用执法之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1155547_comment'></div>夫法吏者，奉行其法可也，宁制法之人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1155547_comment'></div>古人有言，治国如治家，耕当问奴，织当问婢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1155547_comment'></div>今欲与法吏谋致治之本意，是犹使奴织而婢耕，其成功不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1155547_comment'></div>臣欲乞专委鸿博之老及辅弼大臣，商较敕条，略依律文为体，裁其辞句，第其轻重，约其义，明其文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1155547_comment'></div>布之四海，使识朝廷之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1155547_comment'></div>传之万世，俾知文雅之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1155547_comment'></div>自今以往，有臣庶上言，欲釐改旧法，建设条禁者，愿陛下慎其俞旨，必先付之两府，参之群吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1155547_comment'></div>若前条确见其短，今文率以为便，可行于经久者，即下两制，令以所陈之状，去其芜杂，取其精意，仿古律令，著为章程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1155547_comment'></div>若其事止苛文，不足发明利害者，皆寝而勿报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1155547_comment'></div>如此则法不数变，而民知所措矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1155547_comment'></div>言者必难臣曰：今若依律令以为敕，天下官吏必不能晓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1155547_comment'></div>臣对曰：今天下所颁律令，曹局小吏，犹能引用，则似律之敕，独不能晓耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1155547_comment'></div>此胶柱之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1155547_comment'></div>又必难臣曰：夫诏敕者多先帝所定，而不当改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1155547_comment'></div>臣对曰：凡诏敕之设，本臣庶上陈之见耳，宁一出先帝之口哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1155547_comment'></div>况圣人以便利万物为至仁，不因循陈迹为至孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1155547_comment'></div>且太宗皇帝改建隆之敕，真宗皇帝革兴国之法，是皆可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1155547_comment'></div>此守株之谈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1155547_comment'></div>臣又闻「事不师古」，商典实讥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1155547_comment'></div>「必也正名」，鲁堂攸训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1155547_comment'></div>虽文质异尚，沿袭有宜，至于辨尊卑，分职业，其实一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1155547_comment'></div>窃见国朝故事，自使相及左右仆射以上，出典州郡者，皆曰判；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1155547_comment'></div>六尚书、节度使以下者，皆曰知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1155547_comment'></div>盖以谓仆射而上，品秩隆重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1155547_comment'></div>藩镇之任，地望卑远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1155547_comment'></div>故以尊临卑者判其事，以小任大者知其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1155547_comment'></div>及除佐官则例曰同判之职，自京官以上，皆可任焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1155547_comment'></div>今六尚书知州于上，京官判州于下，名既不顺，理亦无稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1155547_comment'></div>而又朝廷之仪，台省为重，近缘茍且，寖失典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1155547_comment'></div>尚书都省，尚书令之职也，今两省五品以上皆得权判；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1155547_comment'></div>刑部流内铨，皆尚书侍郎之职，今或以知杂御史判铨事，或以升朝官判刑曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1155547_comment'></div>其馀卿监之司，小官判者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1155547_comment'></div>天下友邦大郡，大臣不得判；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1155547_comment'></div>天台帝省，小臣得判之，是重诸侯之藩，而轻天子之吏，臣窃以为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1155547_comment'></div>又府史者，二人之名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1155547_comment'></div>故自《周礼》至唐令，有其任者皆曰府若干人，史若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1155547_comment'></div>今寺监见有其人，则并称府史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1155547_comment'></div>此虽小吏而名不师古，亦朝廷之所惜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1155547_comment'></div>幸陛下诏有司按前典，谬者正之，颠者序之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1155547_comment'></div>虽未能复治古之法，亦一时之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1155547_comment'></div>右臣所怀狂瞽，悉已条述，惟陛下裁幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1155547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　本年，在京迁左正言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年1月16日</a>　正月十六日，在京为左正言，受诏权同知贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年4月6日</a>　四月六日，在京为左正言，与章得象等联名进呈，乞赐召试黄庠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年4月</a>　四月，在京擢知制诰，判登闻检院，代郑向看详删定天禧以来诸司编敕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年4月</a>　四月，在京任知制诰，作王绍等推恩赠官制。作品：天平军节度使检校太师同中书门下平章事判河南府王曾男太常寺太祝绍可将作监丞礼部尚书知亳州晏殊男明远可秘书省校书郎资政殿学士尚书户部侍郎薛奎亲侄男房孺可将作监主簿尚书户部侍郎知庐州陈尧佐亲孙男知愚可将作监主簿尚书户部侍郎知永兴军范雍亲孙男子初可将作监主簿翰林侍读学士兼龙图阁学士尚书工部侍郎权知开封府程琳堂弟温瑜可试将作监主簿制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1155185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天平军节度使检校太师同中书门下平章事判河南府王曾男太常寺太祝绍可将作监丞礼部尚书知亳州晏殊男明远可秘书省校书郎资政殿学士尚书户部侍郎薛奎亲侄男房儒可将作监主簿尚书户部侍郎知庐州陈尧佐亲孙男知愚可将作监主簿尚书户部侍郎知永兴军范雍亲孙男子初可将作监主簿翰林侍读学士兼龙图阁学士尚书工部侍郎权知开封府程琳堂弟温瑜可试将作监主簿制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155185")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155185'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155185'>敕：具官王曾男绍等，禀和令胄，服业素风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155185_comment'></div>率在妙龄，未参初仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155185_comment'></div>适因诞节，旅集庆仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155185_comment'></div>乘嘉会之均休，复乃亲之言念，愿延赏典，以启荣阶，循厥旧章，俾覃涣渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155185_comment'></div>卿曹书省，正秩试官，差序以升，勿忘祗勖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155185_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1155185_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年6月16日</a>　六月十六日，在京任知制诰，受诏就秘阁考试制科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年闰6月4日</a>　闰六月四日，在京任知制诰，受诏与张观、李淑编三馆、秘阁书籍，是时已兼史馆修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年闰6月</a>　闰六月，在京任知制诰，上疏建议制科与武举分试，并命有司设幕供饮馔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年9月</a>　九月，在京任知制诰，有诗挽晁迥。作品：赠太子太保晁文公挽词二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_4_106578_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106577?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年11月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106577'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106577'>恩告偃衡荜，年华飞琯灰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106577'>右眠安佛胁，深息养仙胎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106577'>数犯稽违禁，谁怜游落材。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106577_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106577'>使轺均病粟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，更自冁然咍。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年2月13日</a>　二月十三日，在京任知制诰，作王随除知枢密院事制书。作品：参知政事王随除尚书吏部侍郎知枢密院制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1155086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参知政事王随除尚书吏部侍郎知枢密院制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155086")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155086'>敕：国家法象紫枢，总揽皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155086_comment'></div>建为使范，均厥宰司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155086_comment'></div>必求经世之贤，参图基命之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155086_comment'></div>我有公议，属于名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155086_comment'></div>具官王随，器涵虚明，道与和正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155086_comment'></div>感会先帝，摅发懿猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155086_comment'></div>擢高妙之哲科，贲文思之休运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155086_comment'></div>荐阶膴仕，入服大僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155086_comment'></div>自朕震坊之初，尝膺望苑之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155086_comment'></div>逮于纂绍，固已延登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155086_comment'></div>松寒后凋，井德无改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155086_comment'></div>向由近侍，升赞元钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155086_comment'></div>名实具瞻，政亦惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155086_comment'></div>眷乃本兵之地，宜咨同体之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155086_comment'></div>是用陟天官之贰卿，干筹幄之几事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155086_comment'></div>顺考古道，对扬王休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155086_comment'></div>矧试政之已彰，讵锡命而多训？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155086_comment'></div>往践厥位，永保令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155086_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1155086_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年2月13日</a>　二月十三日，在京任知制诰，作李咨除知枢密院事制书。作品：同知枢密院李咨除尚书户部侍郎知枢密院制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1155085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同知枢密院李咨除尚书户部侍郎知枢密院制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155085")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155085'>敕：国家总右武之柄，慎惟几之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155085_comment'></div>号为皇枢，以经天縡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155085_comment'></div>非有明达之懿，畴干宥密之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155085_comment'></div>矧道推同寅，绩昭已试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155085_comment'></div>宜偕上著，用鬯大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155085_comment'></div>具官李咨，器采忠纯，业履宏劭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155085_comment'></div>亮节坚于石席，明履协于蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155085_comment'></div>仰惟先朝，擢在荣序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155085_comment'></div>启迪言选，藻润帝谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155085_comment'></div>肆朕纂临，益俾亲近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155085_comment'></div>递宣方岳之政，再笼天下之财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155085_comment'></div>爰图累劳，参赞基命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155085_comment'></div>百汰无耗，屡照不疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155085_comment'></div>休问日升，众事寖允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155085_comment'></div>是用进地官之亚列，付皇极之秘机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155085_comment'></div>寖陟上司，以辅予治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155085_comment'></div>方今四鄙弗警，五刃并櫜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155085_comment'></div>复兹明哲之才，交修朝夕之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155085_comment'></div>何烦训敕，往服宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155085_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1155085_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年9月12日</a>　九月十二日，在京任知制诰，受诏为《史记》、《汉书》详定官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年11月15日</a>　十一月十五日，在京任知制诰，在圜丘祭典上奉引仁宗升坛赞礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年8月11日</a>　八月十一日，在京任知制诰，受诏为契丹生辰使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　秋，在京任知制诰，兼知审刑院，奏请御史详查王蒙正案。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='637348dcf2d3493fb2b0fc1080c4ca02_label'><a href='javascript:
