ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1041')">1036-1041年</a>，41-46岁</div><div id='637348dcf2d3493fb2b0fc1080c4ca02' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　本年，在京任知制诰，作司马池授三司户部副使制。作品：尚书工部郎中兼侍御史知杂事司马池可三司户部副使制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1155039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书工部郎中兼侍御史知杂事司马池可三司户部副使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155039")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155039'>敕：国家底慎邦财，兼崇使范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155039_comment'></div>以主计之重订于列侯，因制用之副均于小宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155039_comment'></div>非有干用，畴允恪居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155039_comment'></div>以尔具官司马池，行淳而方，识简而固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155039_comment'></div>繇乡俊以来仕，积吏阀而登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155039_comment'></div>荐剖州符，远将岁漕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155039_comment'></div>比嘉守土之最，茂赞操筹之烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155039_comment'></div>朕察其冲恬，考以名实，亟正郎位，俾亚宪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155039_comment'></div>时序甫移，品式方属，而户版缺任，庭著择材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155039_comment'></div>虽纠劾未尽其能，且甄升适在其次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155039_comment'></div>特回簪笔之选，用经笼货之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155039_comment'></div>往竭乃诚，无忝荣遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155039_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1155039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年3月25日</a>　三月二十五日，在京任知制诰，兼判鸿胪寺，奏请外夷朝贡时，问其国邑风俗、道途远近，图其人物衣冠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年9月</a>　九月，在京任知制诰，兼知审刑院，与宰相陈尧佐争，论密州豪右王澥当死。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年10月5日</a>　十月五日，在京任知制诰，受命权判吏部流内铨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　冬，在京任知制诰，奏罢因灾异开寺观祈福事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　冬，在京任知制诰，迁尚书刑部员外郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　本年，在京任知制诰，作司马池授三司度支副使制。作品：三司度支副使尚书工部郎中陈琰可三司盐铁副使三司户部副使尚书工部郎中司马池可三司度支副使制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1155037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三司度支副使尚书工部郎中陈琰可三司盐铁副使三司户部副使尚书工部郎中司马池可三司度支副使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155037")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155037'>敕：故事邦计分部，设使介以经其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155037_comment'></div>虽职任均重，而班著有次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155037_comment'></div>因劳序升，实本其次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155037_comment'></div>以尔具官陈琰性理纯壹，靖而能干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155037_comment'></div>以尔具官司马池器职详允，和而不流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155037_comment'></div>并饰文来仕，展体首公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155037_comment'></div>簪笔握兰，分契将漕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155037_comment'></div>休有嘉绩，稔厥外朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155037_comment'></div>顷偕命于使烦，同胥协以陈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155037_comment'></div>属乃比局，畴以外迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155037_comment'></div>俾按循阶之常，且资奏刀之熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155037_comment'></div>正郎旧秩，会府剧曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155037_comment'></div>各懋尔官，以称恩典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155037_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1155037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年3月1日</a>　三月一日，在京任知制诰，擢为翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年3月</a>　三月，在京为翰林学士，受命为进士殿试考官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年4月</a>　四月，在京为翰林学士，以李淑之谮，未得任同知枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年4月</a>　四月，在京为翰林学士，作赐柴宗庆乞朝觐上寿不允诏。作品：赐武成军节度使同中书门下平章事驸马都尉柴宗庆乞朝觐上寿不允诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐武成军节度使同中书门下平章事驸马都尉柴宗庆乞朝觐上寿不允诏</a><span "poem_title_1155289")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155289'>卿皇室近姻，重侯茂阀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155289_comment'></div>早持帅节，兼视台华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155289_comment'></div>择分陕之名区，寄屏周之良翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155289_comment'></div>会余庆节，遽剡奏封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155289_comment'></div>愿饬介圭之朝，因陪寿斝之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155289_comment'></div>诚虽输向，礼实重烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155289_comment'></div>况任贡已列于前，抚封方倚于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155289_comment'></div>宜绥阃政，昭副朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155289_comment'></div>眷是寅恭，靡忘嘉叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155289_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1155289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年4月</a>　四月，在京为翰林学士，作赐李迪乞赴阙上寿不允诏。作品：赐刑部尚书知徐州李迪乞赴阙上寿不允诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐刑部尚书知徐州李迪乞赴阙上寿不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155290")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155290'>敕李迪：省所上表，乞暂赴阙随班上寿事具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155290_comment'></div>卿久服荩臣，荐持魁柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155290_comment'></div>向当周衮之重，移殿徐邦之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155290_comment'></div>克布惠和，以式方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155290_comment'></div>虽甘棠流咏于陕服，灵河蒙福于汉京，树善相均，配古无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155290_comment'></div>属余诞节，时阅奏封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155290_comment'></div>愿集奉觞之辰，且纾恋阙之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155290_comment'></div>然倚瞩旧老，倡率守麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155290_comment'></div>风化所期，内外惟一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155290_comment'></div>无烦趋觐，姑穆翰垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155290_comment'></div>恭爱之诚，叹赏徒切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155290_comment'></div>所请宜不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155290_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155290_comment'></div>夏热，卿比安好？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155290_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1155290_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年4月</a>　四月，在京为翰林学士，作赐杨崇勋为移知陈州乞朝觐不允诏。作品：赐河阳三城节度使杨崇勋为移知陈州乞朝觐不允诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155292' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155292'>卿早秉戎旄，屡绥藩政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155292_comment'></div>民谣载路，岁筦亟淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155292_comment'></div>向因宛道之夷，后徙淮阳之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155292_comment'></div>隐然屏翰，陪余京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155292_comment'></div>遽阅囊封，愿先载觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155292_comment'></div>眷心存之虽切，顾外倚之有初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155292_comment'></div>无烦造朝，且重分阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155292_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1155292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年4月</a>　四月，在京为翰林学士，作赐赵元昊诏。作品：赐西平王赵元昊为赐差来人见辞例物诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐西平王赵元昊为赐差来人见辞例物诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155294")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155294'>卿志凝忠概，世缵武勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155294_comment'></div>保障有劳，恭亮弥罄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155294_comment'></div>比余诞日，首率贡仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155294_comment'></div>差骏产以斯材，旅庆琛而有焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155294_comment'></div>仍嘉亲校，能恪朝规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155294_comment'></div>既阅右牵之良，特渥匪颁之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155294_comment'></div>且昭恩赉，并宠藩维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155294_comment'></div>永念倾虔，尤增叹尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155294_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1155294_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年6月16日</a>　六月十六日，在京为翰林学士诰，受诏就秘阁考试制科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年7月3日</a>　七月三日，在京为翰林学士，作南郊御札。作品：宝元元年南郊御札敕内外文武臣僚等。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宝元元年南郊御札敕内外文武臣僚等</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年7月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155271")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155271'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155271'>夫一阳大报，方册彝规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155271_comment'></div>三岁亲郊，祖宗盛则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155271_comment'></div>朕猥以凉菲，获承基绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155271_comment'></div>祗率丕训，茂昭前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155271_comment'></div>兢兢业业，罔或宁暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155271_comment'></div>赖上穹鉴祐，列圣保绥，方隅晏然，气物时若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155271_comment'></div>民微艰食之阻，邦辑阜财之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155271_comment'></div>嗣洽太和，莫非灵贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155271_comment'></div>虽复牺币有品，粢芼载蠲，申敕祠官，谨修岁事，然斋辂停轸，钦柴辍熏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155271_comment'></div>弗躬于行，抚己成阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155271_comment'></div>祭疏则怠，心焉增惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155271_comment'></div>矧紫营在望，奚敢惮勤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155271_comment'></div>黄流并祼，庶几能飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155271_comment'></div>爰诹景至之吉，恭迓帝临之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155271_comment'></div>慎举鸿仪，式先诞告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155271_comment'></div>朕以今年十一月十八日有事于南郊，咨尔攸司，各扬乃职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155271_comment'></div>凡所以供调，毋黩典常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155271_comment'></div>应诸道州府，不得以进奉为名，别行科歛，裕神约礼，称朕意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155271_comment'></div>故兹札示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1155271_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年7月</a>　七月，在京为翰林学士，作赐王曾乞南郊陪位不允诏。作品：赐资政殿大学士尚书左仆射判郓州王曾乞南郊陪位不允诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155287' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155287'>卿儒苑上才，公槐隽老，冠名秘殿，均逸东藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155287_comment'></div>虽挹道均冲，而协恭无懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155287_comment'></div>属升禋之诞告，遽剡牍以斯闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155287_comment'></div>愿肃朝銮，旅陪祠鬯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155287_comment'></div>然坐堂之政，甫慰氓谣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155287_comment'></div>拥传之勤，重烦耆德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155287_comment'></div>宜辍甘泉之从，姑绍颍川之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155287_comment'></div>其在倾输，徒增叹瞩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1155287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年7月</a>　七月，在京为翰林学士，作赐夏守赟乞南郊陪位不允诏。作品：赐镇海军节度使知澶州夏守赟乞南郊陪位不允诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐镇海军节度使知澶州夏守赟乞南郊陪位不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155288'>卿以拥节之严，守夹河之重，茂宣民政，总训师和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155288_comment'></div>有邻疆饯劳之烦，有堤事缮完之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155288_comment'></div>实惟勋旧，镇乃要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155288_comment'></div>会郊报之在辰，览邮封而沥恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155288_comment'></div>愿陪盛荐，深体忠怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155288_comment'></div>然职在刺条，地陪寰服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155288_comment'></div>宜切圭符之寄，用纾朝宿之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155288_comment'></div>其在叹嘉，靡忘鉴寐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1155288_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年8月</a>　八月，在京为翰林学士，有诗挽李遵勖。作品：赠驸马都尉李和文公挽词二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106988' id='poem_sentence_1_106988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106988'>得疾真无妄，观生遂若休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106988_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106987?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106987'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106987'>北第琴樽歇，东原旌旆飞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106972'>终无三令喜，便集两楹悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106972'>衮职嗟何补，天心感慭遗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106972'>幽泉空漏淎，非复作霖时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/106971?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年11月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106971'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106971'>自昔荣归衮，今兹骇阅川。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106971'>天愁摧柱日，星痛殒箕年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106971'>素履遗儒范，忠谋溢吏篇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106971'>空馀洧乡陌，长似岘碑前。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年11月</a>　十一月，在京为翰林学士，作赐韩亿诏。作品：赐南京留司文武百官尚书吏部侍郎知应天府韩亿等贺南郊礼毕及上尊号受册诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155269' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155269'>钦崇报本，礼重邦经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155269_comment'></div>刻玉崇号，义缘人欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155269_comment'></div>内循寡德，忝举鸿仪，膺福享名，心焉增愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155269_comment'></div>卿近由丞弼，方委保釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155269_comment'></div>率属罄恭，露章驰贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155269_comment'></div>味其辞旨，忠恪兼勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155269_comment'></div>欣叹之怀，寤寐无舍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1155269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年11月</a>　十一月，在京为翰林学士，作赐范雍贺南郊礼毕诏。作品：赐西京留司文武百官资政殿学士尚书吏部侍郎知河南府范雍等贺南郊礼毕诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155270'>长景涓辰，高禋措事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155270_comment'></div>获膺纯嘏，还霈茂恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155270_comment'></div>三灵交欢，咸与欣会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155270_comment'></div>卿属司留钥，虔戒乃僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155270_comment'></div>便道奉章，旅辞致庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155270_comment'></div>情文参允，将顺并照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155270_comment'></div>申阅于兹，叹瞩何已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155270_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1155270_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年11月</a>　十一月，在京为翰林学士，作赐契丹贺正旦使萧傅到贝州茶药诏。作品：赐契丹贺正旦使萧傅到贝州茶药诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155282'>卿奉将邻币，来庆王正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155282_comment'></div>肃邦礼以惟虔，骛使程而匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155282_comment'></div>眷言次舍，式戾方州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155282_comment'></div>不无鞅掌之勤，宜有绥调之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155282_comment'></div>特推优锡，用集至和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155282_comment'></div>谅即钦承，且昭恩赉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155282_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1155282_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年11月</a>　十一月，在京为翰林学士，作赐契丹贺正旦副使韩志德到贝州茶药诏。作品：赐契丹贺正旦副使韩志德到贝州茶药诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐契丹贺正旦副使韩志德到贝州茶药诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155283")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155283'>卿远服使联，参修聘范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155283_comment'></div>款边关而遄往，冒岁律之凄凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155283_comment'></div>缅是勤斯，轸于劳止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155283_comment'></div>杂颁灵品，助拥时休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155283_comment'></div>宜体眷怀，即当祗荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155283_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1155283_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月</a>　十二月，在京为翰林学士，作柴宗庆加恩制。作品：授柴宗庆开府仪同三司依前检校太师同中书门下平章事武成军节度使驸马都尉加食邑实封制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1155242' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155242' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155242?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授柴宗庆开府仪同三司依前检校太师同中书门下平章事武成军节度使驸马都尉加食邑实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155242")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155242_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155242'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155242'>门下：朕丕承先谟，恭恤明祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155242_comment'></div>获执牲币，祗见神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155242_comment'></div>适当拜胙之成，思均与物之况。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155242_comment'></div>矧余右戚，参视贵台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155242_comment'></div>久拥旌旄之雄，时勤屏翰之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155242_comment'></div>不有异数，畴耸庶邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155242_comment'></div>具官柴宗庆，淳固蹈常，柔嘉广业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155242_comment'></div>地承伐阀之旧，才对肃雍之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155242_comment'></div>能兴乃宗，遂膴斯仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155242_comment'></div>以藩侯而奉朝请，多历岁时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155242_comment'></div>因元帅以敦诗书，自恬风素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155242_comment'></div>逮兼槐席之重，出临棠舍之封，允迪惠和，且宣条教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155242_comment'></div>属禋严之诞布，率贡品以惟寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155242_comment'></div>身虽守藩，志则存阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155242_comment'></div>忠劬并劭，戬禄尔宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155242_comment'></div>是用冠文阶之崇，优食采之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155242_comment'></div>茂厥真赋，济于壮猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155242_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155242_comment'></div>天秩之隆，非式礼而奚叙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155242_comment'></div>公餗之荷，惟持满而克安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155242_comment'></div>益服令图，往即荣次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155242_comment'></div>授受之戒，可不勉欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155242_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1155242_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月</a>　十二月，在京为翰林学士，作陈尧佐加食邑实封制。作品：授陈尧佐光禄大夫依前检校太傅同中书门下平章事淮康军节度使加食邑实封制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1155243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授陈尧佐光禄大夫依前检校太傅同中书门下平章事淮康军节度使加食邑实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155243")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155243'>门下：荐诚类帝，所以格三灵之和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155243_comment'></div>均禧拜胙，所以优四海之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155243_comment'></div>倚吾旧老之隽，方制中权之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155243_comment'></div>兼荣铉台，参殿寰服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155243_comment'></div>礼成第赏，朝论攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155243_comment'></div>具官陈尧佐，志意冲夷，风概高劭，抗心希古，学有本原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155243_comment'></div>展体首公，政多缘饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155243_comment'></div>逮事列圣，目为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155243_comment'></div>寖阶谟猷，遂翊机柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155243_comment'></div>洎入正于槐路，实增焕于衮章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155243_comment'></div>向虽内解政枢，宠颁斋钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155243_comment'></div>仍宰庭视品之峻，冠友邦维翰之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155243_comment'></div>贤劳并均，体貌无改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155243_comment'></div>升禋已事，布号崇朝，宜增命数之繁，且昭贶施之普。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155243_comment'></div>崇阶驭贵，多邑衍封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155243_comment'></div>益以实租，会为异渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155243_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155243_comment'></div>天锡之祉，余弗敢专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155243_comment'></div>师佥之谐，畴可虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155243_comment'></div>往虔诞告之宠，益契同寅之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155243_comment'></div>矧在耆明，无假多谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155243_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1155243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月</a>　十二月，在京为翰林学士，作赐陈尧佐加恩诏。作品：赐淮康军节度使同中书门下平章事陈尧佐加恩诰敕诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155285' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155285' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155285?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐淮康军节度使同中书门下平章事陈尧佐加恩诰敕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155285")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155285_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155285'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155285'>卿儒苑上才，槐阶旧老，茂分旄节，陪我寰畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155285_comment'></div>属郊事之方竣，冀灵休之普洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155285_comment'></div>持扬明命，参宠元侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155285_comment'></div>具刻赞章，往荣藩屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155285_comment'></div>仍俾家庭之嗣，奉将诏版之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155285_comment'></div>萃厥恩私，所宜祗荷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1155285_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　冬，在京为翰林学士，与叶清臣有诗书往来。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　本年，在京为翰林学士，作《中书试戒风俗奢靡诏》作品：中书试戒风俗奢靡诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155266' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155266?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书试戒风俗奢靡诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155266")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155266_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155266'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155266'>闻夫古先哲王之御俗也，皆上求天心，下建民极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155266_comment'></div>天道贵质，故敦本以体元；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155266_comment'></div>民情易流，必闲邪而制法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155266_comment'></div>然后能趋富寿之域，开衣食之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155266_comment'></div>至和来臻，大命无泛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155266_comment'></div>国家荷三圣之业，保万方之大，容典饬尽，训戒谆勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155266_comment'></div>然而世道久夷，人心多靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155266_comment'></div>近闻中外颇僭典常，自通邑名都，世家豪姓，竞作浮侈，迭相矜尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155266_comment'></div>珠玉被于服玩，缇绣裛于垣墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155266_comment'></div>雕几岁更，规矩时易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155266_comment'></div>酱藿庖味，山藻室庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155266_comment'></div>靡嗟民力之勤，罔惮邦仪之禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155266_comment'></div>此而是纵，孰不可容！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155266_comment'></div>况曩者神宗亲驾农祠，示稼穑之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155266_comment'></div>真庙深惜上币，严销涂之律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155266_comment'></div>朕皆祗绍祖武，奉行前猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155266_comment'></div>惟尔庶邦，敢忘茂训！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155266_comment'></div>自时以往，咸俾改为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155266_comment'></div>傥轻蹈于匪彝，当一施于重罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155266_comment'></div>布告遐迩，知朕意焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1155266_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　本年，在京为翰林学士，作赐王鬷生日诏。作品：赐参知政事王鬷生日诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155273'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155273'>志局坚明，材猷肃给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155273_comment'></div>向筦斗枢之重，移参鼎餗之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155273_comment'></div>硕画所经，大伦并辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155273_comment'></div>眷言异禀，实纪初辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155273_comment'></div>嘉贤运之有开，宜恩颁之载渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155273_comment'></div>樽醪且旨，庖牺具将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155273_comment'></div>用昭礼食之华，姑集家庭之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155273_comment'></div>体余注赖，往洽燕私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155273_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1155273_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　本年，在京为翰林学士，子充国赐进士出身。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年7月29日</a>　七月二十九日，在京为翰林学士，作赐范雍充鄜延环庆两路沿边经略安抚使诏。作品：振武军节度使知延州范雍充鄜延环庆两路沿边经略安抚使诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐振武军节度使知延州范雍充鄜延环庆两路沿边经略安抚使诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年7月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155295")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155295'>卿干栋名材，筹帷旧望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155295_comment'></div>自付拥旄之任，即临乘障之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155295_comment'></div>蕞尔狡羌，忘我前施，阴连种部，规扰塞垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155295_comment'></div>虽购募有科，而威防难废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155295_comment'></div>再念诰努控遏之会，安化经营之方，节度素分，绥怀莫一，断于朕志，合乃使名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155295_comment'></div>按琐序劳，繄卿为重，已申朝命，驰锡诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155295_comment'></div>俾蚊虻暴集之辰，有兔犬指纵之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155295_comment'></div>宜钦异数，益讲武韬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155295_comment'></div>内安属国之民，外殄反常之犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155295_comment'></div>称余远略，迟乃茂勋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1155295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年7月29日</a>　七月二十九日，在京为翰林学士，作赐夏竦充泾原秦凤两路沿边经略安抚使诏。作品：赐奉宁军节度使就差知泾州夏竦充泾原秦凤两路沿边经略安抚使诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐奉宁军节度使就差知泾州夏竦充泾原秦凤两路沿边经略安抚使诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年7月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155296")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155296'>卿望映民宗，谋参王体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155296_comment'></div>顷从枢幄之旧，移陟师坛之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155296_comment'></div>出镇三秦，并护诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155296_comment'></div>而叛羌各种，狡穴野心，窃号背恩，游魂伺隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155296_comment'></div>比虽申严边锁，换补将屯，然自平凉以东，陇道交属，建防制要，当在临泾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155296_comment'></div>虑烽燧之警秋，或狂狡之送死，必先威御，以便指纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155296_comment'></div>余心念焉，无易卿者，已颁成命，即俾改辕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155296_comment'></div>特新使号之华，再袭戎铃之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155296_comment'></div>仍令两道，同禀善经，绥御所资，等威皆绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155296_comment'></div>宜钦慎选，毋或惮行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155296_comment'></div>勉壮厥猷，用恢西略。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1155296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年7月</a>　七月，在京为翰林学士，作赐夏守赟生日生饩诏。作品：赐知枢密院夏守赟生日生饩诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155274' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155274' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155274?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐知枢密院夏守赟生日生饩诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155274")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155274_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155274'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155274'>盟府旧勋，枢庭新望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155274_comment'></div>高猷伊始，备赐惟常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155274_comment'></div>矧秋籥之孟辰，纪庆弧之善旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155274_comment'></div>特推蕃锡，且志同寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155274_comment'></div>往洽宴私，谅钦眷待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155274_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1155274_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年9月</a>　九月，在京为翰林学士，作赐陈执中生日生饩诏。作品：赐同知枢密院陈执中生日生饩诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。《元宪集》卷二七《赐同知枢密院陈执中生日生饩诏》，包含二件诏书，当为两年中之作。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年9月</a>　九月，在京为翰林学士，作赐张士逊生日礼物诏。作品：赐宰臣张士逊生日礼物。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1155398' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155398' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155398?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐宰臣张士逊生日礼物</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155398")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155398_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155398'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155398'>卿等业茂承明，望崇辅弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155398_comment'></div>爰属生贤之旦，实昭命世之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155398_comment'></div>宜渥宠颁，用将庆祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155398_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1155398_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　秋，在京为翰林学士，作赐唂厮啰诏。作品：赐罝勒斯赉诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐罝勒斯赉诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155297")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155297'>近者夏州僭逆元昊，孤背朝恩，窃为僭制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155297_comment'></div>已诏有司，应元昊在身官爵及所赐旧姓，并令除削讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155297_comment'></div>卿性资忠勇，世嫉仇雠，得此布闻，谅增同愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155297_comment'></div>然恐元昊恃其凶狡，妄肆侵凌，卿宜先事为防，因机伺便，整扬劲骑，率励众心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155297_comment'></div>或蹑其空虚，出其不意，以时掩击，殄灭丑徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155297_comment'></div>助天道之祸淫，成王威之禁暴，则崇名厚赏，非卿而谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155297_comment'></div>勉建殊勋，副余外御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155297_comment'></div>兼昨者里玻默里乌进奉到阙，言卿有男辖戬、玛克占觉二人，特以卿故，并授团练使，仍支请受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155297_comment'></div>续据秦州奏，得卿文字，知辖戬等各往宗噶尔城并兰州住坐，兼言道不与元昊往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155297_comment'></div>如元昊入汉界，兄弟二人将兵杀截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155297_comment'></div>此盖卿从来一心向国，致辖戬等如此忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155297_comment'></div>况卿父子至亲，义须和协，与卿同共掩杀僭逆元昊，勿落元昊奸便，别致间谋诱引。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1155297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　秋，在京为翰林学士，作赐瞎毡敕书。作品：赐罝勒斯赉男辖戬敕书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1155315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐罝勒斯赉男辖戬敕书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155315")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155315'>敕辖戬：省秦凤路部署司奏，据汝将到蕃字译作汉字，称汝告秦州部署诸官员，自家要抵敌草寇，便各往宗噶尔城并兰州住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155315_comment'></div>蕃汉两家往来，道不与草寇往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155315_comment'></div>如有草寇兵士入汉界来时，自家兄弟二人，将兵士杀伊草寇事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155315_comment'></div>汝款塞踰诚，举宗效顺，奉宣王略，式遏边虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155315_comment'></div>愤狡寇之陆梁，谋成师之犄角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155315_comment'></div>忠怀壮节，朕甚嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155315_comment'></div>然汝兄弟既奉朝廷，即须父子和协，尽心孝顺，和为一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155315_comment'></div>使出兵之时，手足相应，同杀僭逆元昊，斯为上计，勿听奸人间谍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155315_comment'></div>今赐某物，至可领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155315_comment'></div>故兹将谕，想宜知悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155315_comment'></div>秋凉，汝比好否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155315_comment'></div>遣书，指不多及。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1155315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年10月</a>　十月，在京为翰林学士，为曹玮作墓志铭。作品：宋故推诚翊戴功臣彰武军节度延州管内观察处置等使金紫光禄大夫检校太傅使持节都督延州诸军事延州刺史兼御史大夫上柱国武威郡开国公食邑六千五百户食实封一千六百户赠侍中曹公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_1155599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故推诚翊戴功臣彰武军节度延州管内观察处置等使金紫光禄大夫检校太傅使持节都督延州诸军事延州刺史兼御史大夫上柱国武威郡开国公食邑六千五百户食实封一千六百户赠侍中曹公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155599")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155599'>宋有忠勋之臣曰武威曹公，在天圣中以宿将持节分督河北军事，屯中山，庚午春正月丁卯，寝疾甍于位，寿五十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155599_comment'></div>讣闻，天子震悼，不视崇德朝两日，以黄门监玺书告第，走命中谒者护其柩还京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155599_comment'></div>后九年，宝元之己卯，其孤等始以龟筮之吉，归窆封树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155599_comment'></div>有诏鸿胪亚卿典丧事，奉常易其名曰武穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155599_comment'></div>冬十月乙酉，具卤簿鼓，吹葬公及其嫡冯掖夫人潘氏于南洛阳之金谷乡尹村原，从大墓，且言顺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155599_comment'></div>先是其家合官牒世谱以状咨史氏，请辞刻石，让不遂，乃䌷而叙焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155599_comment'></div>公讳玮，字宝臣，其先晋有清河太守泓去官寄孥，始为郡姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155599_comment'></div>后裔再徙，占数真定之灵寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155599_comment'></div>曾祖讳业，祖讳芸，并遭时俶扰，仕本州为牙门大校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155599_comment'></div>职以世及，功缘地遍，阴迈德美，储为庆灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155599_comment'></div>以至烈考枢密使累赠太师尚书令谥武惠讳彬，以明允笃诚，道参运始，禽吴馘蜀，助平天下，翊亮三圣，卒为元老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155599_comment'></div>谂谋帷幄，溢动旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155599_comment'></div>生极师臣之尊，没从大享之配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155599_comment'></div>显扬追贲，为时第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155599_comment'></div>逮公之克济世美，及昆弟宗门之贵，交荷恤典，丛于先报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155599_comment'></div>故今繇祖而上，皆赠太师、尚书令，又封曾祖于荣，大父于越，俱为国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155599_comment'></div>曾祖妣张氏、祖妣李氏皆累封齐、韩二国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155599_comment'></div>祢庙自始薨饰以济阳郡，再易冀、鲁，并为真王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155599_comment'></div>妣高氏及二刘氏又别以秦、齐、陈三国为汤沐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155599_comment'></div>公即武惠王之第四子也，承是休烈，生而岐嶷，童龀英发，雅为先王所器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155599_comment'></div>至道初，以任为西头供奉官、閤门祗候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155599_comment'></div>党项馀种李继迁盗弄朔方兵，穿塞首鼠，强吏不能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155599_comment'></div>时武惠握机政，太宗面访雄俊，以置边琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155599_comment'></div>久之，辄以公应诏，帝喜曰：「卿有祁午，安遑遑更索耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155599_comment'></div>即日召见，命有司加显秩以俟遣，武惠固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155599_comment'></div>及以本职试守陇西郡，年甫十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155599_comment'></div>公自以见知于父子之际，又为明主所识拔，感激忠孝，遂摅才蕴，由廷臣凡八迁至客省使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155599_comment'></div>其间带高、英、康三州刺史、团练防御使各一，荐领华州，一降容州，皆为观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155599_comment'></div>进主镇国、彰化二军节度观察留后，昭武、彰武两军节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155599_comment'></div>其化条所莅，则戍镇戎军，守渭、邠、秦、莱、青、天雄、孟、兖七藩，而渭、天雄皆再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155599_comment'></div>其瑞璋之总则环庆、真定、泾原三路，皆为兵马都钤辖，鄜延路为副都部署，环庆、真定两路并为都部署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155599_comment'></div>国论所咨，则领宣徽南北院使、署枢密院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155599_comment'></div>命秩之备，则阶三品，勋二品，视官帝傅，兼亚丞相，书社六千三百，实干一千六百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155599_comment'></div>以四字为功号，烜赫光耀，冠映侯籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155599_comment'></div>迹公之策名展体，服劳中外，为国方召，多本西略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1155599_comment'></div>初，继迁逋诛寖久，劫群羌为支辅，苛征暴戮，人思自拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1155599_comment'></div>公之捍萧关也，尽条恩诏绥怀之意，以檄诸部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1155599_comment'></div>部人得书，皆东向感泣，或率众内属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1155599_comment'></div>奸党始离，寇略河湟，诸戎归重弗戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1155599_comment'></div>公短兵鏖石门川上，狡众殆歼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1155599_comment'></div>赵德明初丧凶父，有首罪称藩之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1155599_comment'></div>公以天厌馀孽，宜时平荡，愿帅一队缚竖子以衅鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1155599_comment'></div>驿书言状，虑密计周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1155599_comment'></div>时朝议前已许降，谋弗果用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1155599_comment'></div>扬珠玛哈之族合万馀落乞援内徙，诸将惶惑，未知所受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1155599_comment'></div>公独抚其使，自将劲骑薄天都山，凡三日，尽拥其众，按道徐还，中外服其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1155599_comment'></div>再守渭也，古哩羌寇掠不已，公率所部合支军趣武延咸泊川，鼓行夹击，诸帐皆溃，系牛絷马以万计，遂破灭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1155599_comment'></div>又袭叛姓巴勒臧于平凉，剪其巢窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1155599_comment'></div>自是属国者倚汉与天等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1155599_comment'></div>镇天水也，值罝勒斯赉初盛，挟李遵妖妄，自谓吐蕃贵重，当雄西域，稍并他部，恣睢塞外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1155599_comment'></div>遵乃傍缘故事，上书求「赞普」之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1155599_comment'></div>公密疏以《春秋》许外夷者不一而足，今二羌乌合，而所希无法，宜黜桀骜，以尊国防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1155599_comment'></div>真宗纳焉，但授遵保顺节度制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1155599_comment'></div>后果窥伺边隙，包藏祸心，迫胁小种，扇动豪帅，连营方阵，号称十万，乘虚内奰，浸淫于三都之谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1155599_comment'></div>公率军整旅，背城逆战，斩首千级，获利器杂畜三万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1155599_comment'></div>追北至敦煌，骁将马布札尔耻败，负力复屯野吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1155599_comment'></div>公遣死士数百，夜捣其垒，自相蹂殪，群丑遂奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1155599_comment'></div>古哩羌阴谋累年，规败疆事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1155599_comment'></div>先其未发，扫平庐栅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1155599_comment'></div>因是西南诸姓，皆纳款辕门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1155599_comment'></div>遵、赉震怖，遁还故碛，不敢弯弓而取当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1155599_comment'></div>此式遏制胜之大较。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1155599_comment'></div>故事，边民挟弓矢，皆应募为奔命，斗劳赏薄，人情弗惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1155599_comment'></div>公建言能垦境上旷土者，蠲其租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1155599_comment'></div>春秋耕敛，出州兵以护作，而战者忘死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1155599_comment'></div>渠率内属，恩隆无等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1155599_comment'></div>公请百帐以上比古幢主，次比营司马，赞书拜授，列为王官，而来者知劝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1155599_comment'></div>黠羌杀人，辄以羊马自赎，公按律令除其弊，犯华人者论杀之，馀从其俗，而刑无颇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1155599_comment'></div>秦人田讼，弥岁不解，曹吏投隙，窜易版书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1155599_comment'></div>公审其宿奸，一取质剂为验，亡契者贷其负，使得自占，收脱户千六百，租钱四百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1155599_comment'></div>台符宣告州郡以为后式，而文无害矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1155599_comment'></div>此威怀安利之凡最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1155599_comment'></div>若其按秦汉旧迹，因长城之堑稍筑坞堠，以殊内外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1155599_comment'></div>斥境千里，建笼竿之壁，列弓门十寨，迭为藩蔽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1155599_comment'></div>班赏格，饰斗具，缮梁表道，屯田足食，迄今为保障之利者，不可悉纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1155599_comment'></div>公之在关陇，以威名庄重，渊回山立，累功懋赏，皆即拜稍迁，倚而不召者，岁踰二纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1155599_comment'></div>至于丁外内艰，泣血委印绶，率以墨缞夺服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1155599_comment'></div>天禧中始有下邽观风之拜，犹副戎柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1155599_comment'></div>时三陲宁晏，外虞讫息，佥以公壮猷盛烈，当敷及天下，于是有留使宣猷之授，入筦枢极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1155599_comment'></div>公既践修世范，知无不为，秉义据正，勤劳夙夜，海内抗颂，归《缁衣》之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1155599_comment'></div>终以勋高地偪，更由总管之任，出临西夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1155599_comment'></div>谗党乘胜，又以容山之拜，徙守东藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1155599_comment'></div>圣上始初清明，诛放憸猾，不俟辩谤，寖还旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1155599_comment'></div>奠营丘，藩全魏，养疾明律，兴护北方，再陟斋坛，终屏王室，洪棱劲节，久而弥厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1155599_comment'></div>方且桓圭皂马，伫来朝之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1155599_comment'></div>彤弓彫戈，将蕃锡之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1155599_comment'></div>昊天不吊，歼良奄及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1155599_comment'></div>此哲侯所以深闻鼙之悼，邦人所以寄成蹊之泣者已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1155599_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1155599_comment'></div>公之材之劭本沈雄，而施事干然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1155599_comment'></div>承藉先训，济之谦悫，保功约己，未尝有过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1155599_comment'></div>临政精悍，不独以军旅从事，故数佩州组，皆以最闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1155599_comment'></div>大指道威信，必赏罚，以军之严移于郡，则肃然畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1155599_comment'></div>以郡之爱移于军，则薰然和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1155599_comment'></div>伍符吏牍，参行不慁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1155599_comment'></div>古名将之惮，公优为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1155599_comment'></div>彰后褒勤赏捷，受方底书以数十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1155599_comment'></div>若其询逮兵策，则宝跗细劄，委曲纤悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1155599_comment'></div>甚者手诏往反，如宣帝问后将军故事，决而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1155599_comment'></div>在常赵感疹方革，营卒以常过干军禁，左右劝宽其罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1155599_comment'></div>公曰：「以病易守，非吾节也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1155599_comment'></div>卒置殊死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1155599_comment'></div>故公之约，所守如介石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1155599_comment'></div>公之重，所至为长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1155599_comment'></div>言料敌则焞龟，语应变则奏刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1155599_comment'></div>用能英声茂绩，超盖前代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1155599_comment'></div>行均椒兰之芬，威无藜藿之采，有由然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1155599_comment'></div>论者犹以羌浑右鄙，事微敌脆，不足畅桓桓之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1155599_comment'></div>晚睨幽朔，悲歌慷慨，常谓禅姑衍、铭燕然者，复何人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1155599_comment'></div>时方弭兵，公亦赍志，此又谋夫壮士击剑长怀而不能已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1155599_comment'></div>继室曰沈氏，今号吴兴郡夫人，故相仆射伦之孙，光禄少卿继宗之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1155599_comment'></div>三子，长曰僖，任礼宾副使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1155599_comment'></div>次曰倚，终内殿崇班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1155599_comment'></div>曰英，为供备库副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1155599_comment'></div>噫，门阀隆贵，蝉联鱼贯，以功名世家者，今无偶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1155599_comment'></div>游谈故老，尚将传而不泯，又况图金刻期陵岸，则公之终誉，其有既乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1155599_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_116_1155599'>岩岩常山，灵气磅礴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1155599_comment'></div>值为豪英，拔秀辽廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1155599_comment'></div>洸洸侍中，实本浑熊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1155599_comment'></div>纂服肖善，自箕而弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1155599_comment'></div>武惠知子，献之天扆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1155599_comment'></div>弗啬家宝，用参国器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1155599_comment'></div>党项猖狂，扰宋西疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1155599_comment'></div>公冠未升，戍于秦凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1155599_comment'></div>治兵刺部，或征或抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1155599_comment'></div>游魂残孽，莫敢余侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1155599_comment'></div>婪婪大酋，交兵结仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1155599_comment'></div>率尔蕃部，搏我边州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1155599_comment'></div>公计先定，聊秉武节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1155599_comment'></div>螳臂蛙跗，卒染车辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1155599_comment'></div>蕃族震携，款塞就羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1155599_comment'></div>灭烽卧龙，帝曰来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1155599_comment'></div>计功酬绩，大使方伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1155599_comment'></div>乃干鸿枢，柔惠正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1155599_comment'></div>间因谗人，旋陟旧勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1155599_comment'></div>三偃大藩，再帅中军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1155599_comment'></div>屏于北道，威声偃草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1155599_comment'></div>公侯干城，宜寿宜考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1155599_comment'></div>耳顺未踰，与世长违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1155599_comment'></div>彻我金汤，帝曰予思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1155599_comment'></div>貂廞衮襚，哀荣并至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1155599_comment'></div>宠葬周原，陪先洛涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1155599_comment'></div>俨画柳兮彷徉，公将傃兮幽堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1155599_comment'></div>惟松楸兮嗣世，尚桥梓于家王。</div><div id='poem_sentence_143_1155599_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年11月15日</a>　十一月十五日，在京为翰林学士，拜右谏议大夫、参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年12月12日</a>　十二月十二日，在京为参知政事，上奏唐入阁仪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年闰12月15日</a>　十二月望日，在京为参知政事，有诗。作品：闰十二月望日立春禁中作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_106674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闰十二月望日立春禁中作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年闰12月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106674")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106674'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106674'>闰历先春破腊寒，䌽花金胜宠千官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106674'>水从太液池边动，柳向灵和殿里看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106674'>瑞气因风生禁仗，暖晖依日上仙盘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106674'>须知圣运随生殖，万国年年共此欢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106674'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106674_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　本年，在京为翰林学士，作《敕州郡劝农诏》作品：敕州郡劝农诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕州郡劝农诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155267")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155267'>昔者尧、汤之灾而民不病，知备故也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155267_comment'></div>禹、稷之盛而身服劳，知本故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155267_comment'></div>惟本与备一出于农，哲王尽心，义在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155267_comment'></div>矧去圣愈邈，务本日衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155267_comment'></div>非告以话言，纳之善道，则惧夫懈怠之俗，相靡而弗还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155267_comment'></div>富寿之期，因循而莫复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155267_comment'></div>朕所以躬绍祖武，亲礼农祠，御千亩之场，越三推之数，因以申劳狎野，优复力田，招来太和，茂育群品，则虢公谏宣之旨，贾谊劝文之戒，朕虽不德，庶或无惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155267_comment'></div>而今春以来，善气犹郁，蝗羽为孽，雨足屯膏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155267_comment'></div>南自淮、楚而接之江，东绵齐、鲁而著之海，野乏青草，家无见粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155267_comment'></div>丁壮轻去于里庐，细弱相捐于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155267_comment'></div>会未周岁，奄及大饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155267_comment'></div>至于邦县之间，率寡京坻之蓄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155267_comment'></div>教不先具，民亦何辜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155267_comment'></div>庸非贪吏以掊克而夺其财，苛人以趋办而穷其力，淫巧游惰者失其禁，逮讯證捕者妨其时，使吾赤子陷于饥寒，嘉岁变于禨眚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155267_comment'></div>兴言及此，朕甚痛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155267_comment'></div>况视民之勤，礼存彝训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155267_comment'></div>垦田罔实，汉有明诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155267_comment'></div>自今以还，其申敕诏条，切督州郡，凡令之出，以农为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155267_comment'></div>谨视土膏之宜，明宣稼政之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155267_comment'></div>谕以国家宝谷重食，尊本镇浮，庶几流亡有所底止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155267_comment'></div>敢或弛厥穑事，重为民殃，当一置于重科，俾大变于衰俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155267_comment'></div>布告天下，知朕意焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1155267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　本年，在京为翰林学士，作赐司马池待罪特放诏。作品：赐尚书工部郎中天章阁待制知同州司马池为澄城县百姓党岫持刀刺杀亲叔依条斩讫待罪特放诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1155286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐尚书工部郎中天章阁待制知同州司马池为澄城县百姓党岫持刀刺杀亲叔依条斩讫待罪特放诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155286")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155286'>汉辅要邦，秦馀旧俗，化条所被，恩种宜悛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155286_comment'></div>何兹悖德之氓，靡率怀音之教，毒加亲序，污我人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155286_comment'></div>卿适莅郡封，载钦官狱，耻闻凶类，寻正严诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155286_comment'></div>闭阁示愆，露章引劾，愿任吏师之责，益彰臣礼之恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155286_comment'></div>观过有来，省躬奚咎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155286_comment'></div>勉兴善政，以牧吾民。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1155286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年1月1日</a>　正月一日，在京为参知政事，反对以日食罢宴彻乐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年2月2日</a>　二月二日，在京为参知政事，请于潼关严设守备。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年9月7日</a>　九月七日，在京为参知政事，上奏车驾行幸仪卫事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　本年，在京为参知政事，兼管枢密院机事，上言边帅官重问题。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　春，在京为参知政事，有诗挽宋绶。作品：赠司徒兼侍中宋宣献挽词四首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_106982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106982'>何言隆栋吉，忽叹夜舟藏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_107072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠传法光梵二大卿兼述译场之盛</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107072")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_107072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107072'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107072'>梵劫扶皇历，高才会圣门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107072'>五天真释种<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：传法，北邙土之贵种。）</span>，三国旧王孙<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：光梵，故吴王李氏从子。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107072'>译诂生知慧<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：光梵自童子便通华竺之语。）</span>，卿联万户恩<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107072'>斋熏光汉邸，结集盛秦园。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107072'>交照无殊俗，多闻属上根<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_5_107072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107072'>妙义观心德，华音置使翻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107072'>列圣文垂象<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>，旁行笔记源<sup class='reference 自注：二公虽夷夏有殊，而法性惟一。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_107072_0'>⑶ 自注：光梵奉诏重撰《景祐法宝录》十卷，奏上之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_107072_0'>⑷ ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年2月5日</a>　二月五日，在京任集贤相，与文彦博等上《明堂大飨记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年2月</a>　二月，在京任集贤相，奏杜枢越次言事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年2月</a>　二月，在京任集贤相，被谏官弹劾，上表乞罢相。作品：乞罢相表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢相表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155539")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155539'>臣闻名本戒乎多取，过实则凶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155539_comment'></div>力所贵乎自量，弗能当止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155539_comment'></div>矧万几密勿，任切于论思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155539_comment'></div>一介婆娑，力穷于报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155539_comment'></div>所宜自劾，以警空餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155539_comment'></div>仰赖至仁，罄敷危诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155539_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155539_comment'></div>窃念臣学非全古，才不逮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155539_comment'></div>擢始布衣，进陪书笏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155539_comment'></div>宝元中因缘人乏，参预政机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155539_comment'></div>试可罔功，踰年赐免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155539_comment'></div>已覂之驾，奚望于复骖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155539_comment'></div>方汲之渊，何图于续绠？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155539_comment'></div>自再尘于国论，俄六改于岁阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155539_comment'></div>龊龊备员，容容取诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155539_comment'></div>其间改使枢管，序正宰司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155539_comment'></div>光华所丛，位望弥峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155539_comment'></div>然属边烽罢警，调軵息勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155539_comment'></div>列辟交脩，日新于所治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155539_comment'></div>当宁亲务，天健而愈强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155539_comment'></div>因用具臣，久忝高位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155539_comment'></div>至夫讲求坠典，崇报上神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155539_comment'></div>因大寝之宏规，复九筵之毖祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155539_comment'></div>克成钜礼，莫匪圣谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155539_comment'></div>既绝望于清光，亦奚资于彼相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155539_comment'></div>逮均庆宠，首及庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155539_comment'></div>让爵无阶，履高增慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155539_comment'></div>重以福基素狭，年事日侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155539_comment'></div>有负乘之近忧，乏将明之远业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155539_comment'></div>虽主恩含垢，外弭于人言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155539_comment'></div>而天道害盈，难逃于鬼瞰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155539_comment'></div>一岁之内，二息云亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155539_comment'></div>昧圣哲忘情之高，深朋友离群之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155539_comment'></div>气衰耳塞，泪热目昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155539_comment'></div>寂听则妖鼓乱聪，审视则黑花盈睫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1155539_comment'></div>居多忘误，动辄震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1155539_comment'></div>悲忧一来，志虑俱耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1155539_comment'></div>安可尚联衮职之贵，分揖槐庭之严？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1155539_comment'></div>身不自聊，政于何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1155539_comment'></div>且三公之责吏事，任靡容私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1155539_comment'></div>圣主之督愚臣，悔将累国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1155539_comment'></div>内循非据，实玷具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1155539_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下念禀数之早奇，悯匪才之难强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1155539_comment'></div>许还重柄，出补外藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1155539_comment'></div>爱小器于未盈，免其必覆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1155539_comment'></div>贷槁骸于将陨，俾遂更生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1155539_comment'></div>进退之方，恩义偕允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1155539_comment'></div>投诚无隐，须可为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1155539_comment'></div>臣无任祈天俟命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1155539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155539'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷四一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155539_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年3月9日</a>　三月九日，在京任集贤相，因再被谏官弹劾，罢相，出知河南府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年3月13日</a>　三月十三日，在京，诏立班在观文殿学士前。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年3月</a>　三月，在京任集贤相，荐举王畴。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c5017a57890b4562be2cf0e76f1420ae_label'><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107149'>子昔久蒙润，逢辰亨乃嘉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107149'>联飞奉台阁，相顾引龟緺。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107149'>鲍叔不予怯，楚臣宁汝瑕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107149'>时过蒋生径，或诣子云家。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107149'>柏将松并悦，人与室非遐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107149'>君命良不淑，浮生兹有涯。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107149'>沈疴犯霜露，幽谶发龙蛇。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107149'>美志一朝尽，馀哀千古赊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_106673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106673'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106673'>晓出西郊道，回瞻北阙天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106673'>城头云敛盖，关外月低弦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　约于本年，在京任枢密使，荐范纯仁试馆职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年4月3日</a>　四月三日，在京任枢密使，受命为祫享太庙仪仗使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月17日</a>　十月十七日，在京任枢密使，以祫享太庙礼成，进封莒国公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年4月25日</a>　四月二十五日，在京任枢密使，与程戡不协，致其罢枢密副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年11月</a>　十一月，在京任枢密使，受吕诲、赵抃等弹劾，上表乞罢。作品：乞罢枢相表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢枢相表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155538")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155538'>臣闻器小易盈者难持，任重将颠者思止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155538_comment'></div>傥奉承之有失，即陨越之可虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155538_comment'></div>敢援至言，冒陈丹蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155538_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃念臣早由谨朴，参备丞疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155538_comment'></div>出入践扬，二十馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155538_comment'></div>食浮日积，官谤愈諠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155538_comment'></div>而自再冠洪枢，渐逼衰景；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155538_comment'></div>徒竭短虑，终误远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155538_comment'></div>故经制边陲，或蛮蜑内侮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155538_comment'></div>按列军伍，或戍卒未充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155538_comment'></div>上资圣谟，并禀成算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155538_comment'></div>至于稍严赏格，则群喣漂山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155538_comment'></div>暂塞倖门，则众怨成府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155538_comment'></div>孤特少助，怯懦自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155538_comment'></div>敢窃天工，久妨贤路？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155538_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下许还重柄，垂丐残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155538_comment'></div>得宽典刑，庶保要领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155538_comment'></div>傥未令便归田里，或且许近守藩州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155538_comment'></div>补报之心，内外惟一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155538_comment'></div>投诚至切，得请为期。<div class='inline' -----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f01521880ce34348aa545df9a77994a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f01521880ce34348aa545df9a77994a2");'><span id='f01521880ce34348aa545df9a77994a2_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　本年，在襄州通判任，有诗述怀。作品：初倅襄阳郡事感而自咏三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_106424' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106424' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106424?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初倅襄阳郡事感而自咏三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1024年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106424")'>宋庠</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_1_106424_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106424'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_106424_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106423' class='authorDate'>（1024年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_106423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106423'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106423'>诏版熏芝矞露浓，千龄华旦此亲逢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106423'>平刑六百叨优秩<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：汉廷尉平六百石秩。）</span>，已愧琅邪邴曼容。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106423'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_106423_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106422?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106422'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106422'>处世儒宫井臼贫，偶怀铜刻逐观宾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106422'>汉家衒鬻盈千数，却用淄川牧豕人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106422'></div><div -----title
扬州（江都）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='83b0e33db41845bfb635d57c193b4a93_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("83b0e33db41845bfb635d57c193b4a93");'><span id='83b0e33db41845bfb635d57c193b4a93_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1042')">1041-1042年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='83b0e33db41845bfb635d57c193b4a93' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　夏，到知扬州任，有谢表。作品：扬州谢到任表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>扬州谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155524")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155524'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155524'>淮海奥区，圭符假守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155524_comment'></div>扬舲戒道，止涉安流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155524_comment'></div>引绂睹章，即颁圣诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155524_comment'></div>舟毂一都之会，夫家万室之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155524_comment'></div>去国匪遥，偃藩何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155524_comment'></div>臣某诚荣诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155524_comment'></div>伏念臣禀姿蒙拙，陶化亨嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155524_comment'></div>始擢草茅，寖阶缨襘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155524_comment'></div>斗筲量浅，丞史愿微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155524_comment'></div>常蹈道以自安，敢越思而希进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155524_comment'></div>猥由文馆，入忝词垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155524_comment'></div>俄自禁扃，召参台府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155524_comment'></div>此际清衷素定，靡复类能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155524_comment'></div>群议虽諠，罔容收涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155524_comment'></div>因怀自励，讫称大恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155524_comment'></div>而浅谋不足以计深，愚虑妄思夫效智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155524_comment'></div>叛羌负德，边上宿兵，亟会宰司，参图戎索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155524_comment'></div>庙堂集论，或率己而妄言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155524_comment'></div>帷幄定谋，卒因人而免悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155524_comment'></div>曾微寸效，可益万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155524_comment'></div>至于进策治朝，敷言庶位，纤悉咸资于睿断，周旋莫企于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155524_comment'></div>备位踰年，妨贤积日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155524_comment'></div>虽官箴挈矩，仅守匹夫之廉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155524_comment'></div>而公路须才，安称明君之蓄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155524_comment'></div>加以惷冥自禀，濩落少机，言或漏于属垣，疑多成于纳履，积为怨咎，仰玷和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155524_comment'></div>矧当责实之辰，宜被黜幽之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155524_comment'></div>伏遇皇帝陛下兼容如地，载照为春，尽赦多尤，止停贰职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155524_comment'></div>仍七人之旧列，总千骑于大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155524_comment'></div>假以便安，纾其惴慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155524_comment'></div>顾微生之再造，滨十死以何辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155524_comment'></div>谨当歛分思愆，首公营职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155524_comment'></div>因楚人之既教，济汉令之在宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155524_comment'></div>乘乃化孚，期于政辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155524_comment'></div>然念操心易感，实本于孤臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155524_comment'></div>求旧与归，更依于仁后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1155524_comment'></div>视风波而累息，傃丝路以迷魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1155524_comment'></div>临启怔忪，心随涕陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1155524_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1155524_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155524'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155524_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　夏，到知扬州任后，有诗自省。作品：淮南自讼。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_106919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮南自讼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106919")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106919'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106919'>偶然人乏贰中枢，赐罢犹专督府居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106919'>发白自伤闻道晚，心丹谁识报恩馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106919'>淮天目极风帆驶，韩野魂销宰树疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106919'>却顾病身何所用，只堪归钓颍滩鱼。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　秋，在知扬州任，游扬州大明寺，有诗。作品：游大明寺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_107165' class='_poem'><div
