id='poem_title_107165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107165'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107165'>总辔出西坰，寥寥旭宇明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107165'>丛冈森地秀，飞塔恍神行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107165'>惠味沾仙露，疲心识化城。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107165'>远香来不断，空梵过犹清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107165'>坐惜忘机晚，居惭緤组荣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107165'>抚怀今古恨，高世友僚情。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107165'>顾慕群芳歇，徘徊极野平。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107165'>低云参驻盖，寒木隐前旌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107165'>风转松添韵，霜馀菊挫英。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107165'>碧垂天势匝，红上日华轻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107165'>垒废麇麚乐，池荒雁鹜鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107165'>宫垣除濞国<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：伪吴故宫在此。）</span>，台址畏轩兵<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：建隆行阙据其内。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107165'>胜践欣同适，沈忧悔自婴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_107165'>理融无物我，神照罢将迎。<div id='poem_sentence_13_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_107165'>绚藻春供丽，投珍佩合声。<div id='poem_sentence_14_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_107165'>莫嗤三叹拙，聊谢两心倾。<div id='poem_sentence_15_107165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_107165'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_107165_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　秋，在知扬州任，登扬州大明寺塔，有诗。作品：登大明寺塔。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　秋，在知扬州任，朝谒扬州建隆寺，有诗。作品：朝谒建隆寺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span>建隆寺北池亭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝谒建隆寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_106940'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106940'>郡国高皇庙，天龙释帝居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106940'>兵销擒布后，台耸畏轩馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106940'>宝榻成莲坐<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：其寺中有当时御榻。）</span>，戎韬入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_106940", 106940, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>贝书</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106940'>守臣荣就望，屏息拜前除。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106940_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建隆寺北池亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106731")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106731'>宝刹开初地，沧浪绕故城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106731'>芰莲俱野色，凫鸨各秋声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106731'>岸阔烟无著，窗虚日易明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106731'>归骖谁讶久，正为濯尘缨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　秋，在知扬州任，游扬州山光寺，有诗。作品：季秋晓出题山光寺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全宋诗》卷二〇一。）</span><div id='poem_107121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_107121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>季秋晓出题山光寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_107121")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_107121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107121'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107121'>旦夕人语喧，汎舟北城曲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107121'>十里望禅刹，飘若尘外躅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107121'>是日秋宇高，清辉澹晨旭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107121'>林风唱残蜩，泽稗下饥鹄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107121'>野实迎露黄，川芜傲霜绿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_107121'>循涯得微径，舍楫步幽麓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_107121'>佛寺讶靓深，僧庐互重复。<div id='poem_sentence_6_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_107121'>山气导真想，天香洗烦欲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_107121'>嗟余秉微尚，丘壑返初服。<div id='poem_sentence_8_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_107121'>失计蹈尘嚣，虚名玷缨毂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_107121'>妄排金马门，谬草紫泥牍。<div id='poem_sentence_10_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_107121'>温省专慎辞，中阶佐调餗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_107121'>器偏固自倾，绠短良难续。<div id='poem_sentence_12_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_107121'>何言一麾出，尚参九州牧。<div id='poem_sentence_13_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_107121'>恩深无后疵，颜腼有馀恧。<div id='poem_sentence_14_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_107121'>孔训惩惮改，羲爻许频复。<div id='poem_sentence_15_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_107121'>朅来清净区，冀脱泥涂辱。<div id='poem_sentence_16_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_107121'>醉象或可调，藩羝悔前触。<div id='poem_sentence_17_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_107121'>万缘自我空，至道非外勖。<div id='poem_sentence_18_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_107121'>聊谨三载期，吾得事栖伏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_107121'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_107121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_107121'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_107121_0'>⑴ 二句原缺，据清嘉庆《重修扬州府志》卷二八补</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_107121_0'>⑵ 清崔华康熙《重修扬州府志》卷一九</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_107121_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年11月20日</a>　冬至夜，在知扬州任，遥想南郊祭典，有诗。作品：冬至夜斋中不寐遥想郊丘盛礼二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_106379' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106379?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬至夜斋中不寐遥想郊丘盛礼二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106379")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_106379_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106379'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106379'>阳郊陪礼忽三年，目想坛觚切绛烟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106379'>今夕纤萝还不动，百神应到紫宫前<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106379'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_106379_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_106379'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_106379_0'>⑴ 自注：宝元郊祀之夕，风月澄霁，今岁复尔。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_106379_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_106378' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106378' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106378?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年11月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_106378_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106378'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106378'>两扶天御陟圆丘<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，璧月珠星拂䌽旒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106378'>谁识从官兴感夜，卧听寒柝宿扬州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106378'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_106378_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_106378'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_106378_0'>⑴ 自注：景祐、宝元二郊，余并摄公卿，奉引乘舆升坛赞礼。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_106378_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年12月15日</a>　十二月十五日，在知扬州任，因曾提举修《崇文总目》，获加阶及食邑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年12月</a>　十二月，在知扬州任，有谢加恩表。作品：谢《崇文总目》加恩表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢崇文总目加恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155518")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155518'>窃念臣早以片文，误阶荣牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155518_comment'></div>序服星垣之职，入陪銮禁之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155518_comment'></div>凡在官司，多尘总领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155518_comment'></div>爰属仙瀛之藏，广收蠹简之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155518_comment'></div>庋阁寖盈，签题罔辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155518_comment'></div>特迂诏旨，就择时英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155518_comment'></div>俾分讨于艺文，且精求于领目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155518_comment'></div>远袭九流之别，近寻四库之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155518_comment'></div>通质旧章，日程新课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155518_comment'></div>而臣首膺迁擢，最贸岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155518_comment'></div>未终刊谬之功，已忝参机之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155518_comment'></div>缇铅清局，别委于俊僚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155518_comment'></div>山薮宽恩，寻投于外服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155518_comment'></div>逮诸儒之卒业，非孤臣之预知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155518_comment'></div>比者伏蒙皇帝陛下垂览新书，嘉闻善职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155518_comment'></div>追念摩编之久，靡遗尺寸之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155518_comment'></div>爰俾罔功，亦膺蕃数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155518_comment'></div>茂进文阶之品，真疏干食之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155518_comment'></div>愧集荣先，奖浮愿表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155518_comment'></div>上《中经》之簿，莫接于清班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155518_comment'></div>出内史之方，何胜于渥训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155518_comment'></div>仰被烛幽之诏，未知论报之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155518_comment'></div>临启徘徊，言因谢尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155518_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1155518_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155518'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155518_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　冬，在知扬州任，赠梅尧臣双鹅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　约于本年，在知扬州任，误取公使酒，立偿之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　春，在知扬州任，有诗述怀。作品：淮南早春风雨连日俗以为宜。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_106918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮南早春风雨连日俗以为宜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106918")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106918'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106918'>淮海岁方新，层阴便浃辰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106918'>山山能作雨，物物解呈春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106918'>野鸟千声异，江芜一色匀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106918'>农区田溜满，偏慰守藩臣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106918_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106918'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　春，在知扬州任，再游建隆寺，有诗。作品：春晚坐建隆寺北池亭上。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_106465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春晚坐建隆寺北池亭上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_106465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106465'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106465'>城外东风卷落花，更临春水惜年华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106465'>单车刺史无铙吹，叫杀荒池两部蛙<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：南方气早，春末已蛙鸣。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106465_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106465'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_106465_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　秋，在知扬州任，再登大明寺塔，有诗。作品：登大明寺塔。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷二。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　冬，在知扬州任，加资政殿学士，徙知郓州，兼京东西路安抚使，有谢表。作品：谢加职移知郓州表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加职移知郓州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155528")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155528'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155528'>轻轺将命，秘殿参华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155528_comment'></div>易守东藩，治行便道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155528_comment'></div>宠章繁集，愧汗交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155528_comment'></div>臣某诚荣诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155528_comment'></div>窃念臣世系单平，天姿浅固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155528_comment'></div>亲遘尚文之会，首叨擢秀之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155528_comment'></div>因士易农，缘名责实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155528_comment'></div>褫巾未久，通籍为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155528_comment'></div>乘善养于群材，预遍阶于显列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155528_comment'></div>曾微风绩，遂亚疑丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155528_comment'></div>龊龊备员，兢兢履薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155528_comment'></div>物胜权而衡殆，形过鉴而照穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155528_comment'></div>理有固然，道无不踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155528_comment'></div>果烦赐罢，方厌腾讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155528_comment'></div>尚蒙藏疾之仁，寻假出麾之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155528_comment'></div>奄绥淮服，坐服汉条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155528_comment'></div>省咎穷年，酬恩靡日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155528_comment'></div>比者伏蒙皇帝陛下哀怜旧物，收拭深疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155528_comment'></div>念器使之尝加，忍生成而遂弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155528_comment'></div>曲回天造，申穆朝猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155528_comment'></div>序联清禁之崇，再委名城之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155528_comment'></div>仍衔使节，参重州符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155528_comment'></div>恍祗命以惊魂，徒拜嘉而陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155528_comment'></div>桑榆收效，已辱于垂矜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155528_comment'></div>顶踵捐生，未知夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1155528", 1155528, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>上报</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155528_comment'></div>臣见依准敕命，取便路发赴本任，无任瞻仰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1155528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155528'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155528_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
东平（须城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8a423b8e3e5c4a06a243fbb410f87d91_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a423b8e3e5c4a06a243fbb410f87d91");'><span id='8a423b8e3e5c4a06a243fbb410f87d91_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　冬，到知郓州任，有谢表。作品：郓州谢到任表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郓州谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155525")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155525'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155525'>西清秘秩，式宠儒林；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155525_comment'></div>东夏奥区，更均邦翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155525_comment'></div>参为异数，猥集孤臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155525_comment'></div>祗荷甄收，举增惶震<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155525_comment'></div>窃念臣斗筲近器，韦布诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155525_comment'></div>兴于羁旅之馀，玷厥殊科之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155525_comment'></div>向阶华剧，进预疑丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155525_comment'></div>遭百度之交修，乏寸长而上报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155525_comment'></div>久蒙君养，曷逃尸素之惭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155525_comment'></div>终不汝疵，寖累含容之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155525_comment'></div>逮从外补，方涉再期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155525_comment'></div>前忝未酬，来讥已积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155525_comment'></div>敢谓伏蒙皇帝陛下曲全邦体，申奖官成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155525_comment'></div>枉汉札之深辞，易汶田之巨镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155525_comment'></div>冠升殿职，宠映藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155525_comment'></div>仍加别使之名，兼抚连城之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155525_comment'></div>矧惟州部，匪远寰畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155525_comment'></div>津陆交途，农商宿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155525_comment'></div>封峦在望，泽多肤寸之滋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155525_comment'></div>鸣跸如闻，野有储胥之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155525_comment'></div>兹焉寄任，允属循良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155525_comment'></div>退念散材，曷胜优委？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155525_comment'></div>敢不率循丕宪，上体至慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155525_comment'></div>蠲狱市之烦文，济诗书之美俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155525_comment'></div>庶几安辑，少副忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155525_comment'></div>自馀顶踵之微，或效涓埃之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155525_comment'></div>辞殚语拙，感激何云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155525_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1155525_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155525'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155525_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　本年，在知郓州任，捕盗贼，兴郡学，礼师儒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　约于本年，在知郓州任，进给事中，有谢表。作品：谢转给事中表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转给事中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155530")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155530'>邮传疾驰，赞书申锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155530_comment'></div>改东台之秘秩，仍左竹之善藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155530_comment'></div>恩数并隆，心颜罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155530_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃念臣本惟弱植，素懵远猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155530_comment'></div>一玷文科，荐膺朝选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155530_comment'></div>摄官承乏，率非才举之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155530_comment'></div>舍垢匿瑕，阴荷天私之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155530_comment'></div>获遍阶于华近，固无补于涓毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155530_comment'></div>至乃超备谏员，参闻宰政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155530_comment'></div>当求治责成之会，有先机断论之烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155530_comment'></div>力勉徒勤，道悠自踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155530_comment'></div>辱收还于重任，始厌伏于烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155530_comment'></div>继荷宸慈，曲存邦体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155530_comment'></div>旋易麾于巨镇，复帖职于清厢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155530_comment'></div>追贷前尤，丛臻谬宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155530_comment'></div>谢生无所，履薄增忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155530_comment'></div>不谓更枉公佥，平稽岁伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155530_comment'></div>例举当迁之典，兼纡即赏之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155530_comment'></div>循践殊资，俾光外寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155530_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下深怜旧物，均饰庶工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155530_comment'></div>因虞篇陟考之文，用汉守增留之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155530_comment'></div>并推优渥，昭示保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155530_comment'></div>内省微躯，曷胜鸿施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155530_comment'></div>谨当勤思寡悔，益服攸箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155530_comment'></div>承化树风，或万分而有取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155530_comment'></div>竭忠酬贶，期十死以知归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155530_comment'></div>感极于中，辞殚靡喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155530_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1155530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155530'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155530_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　约于本年，在知郓州任，数为京东转运使沈邈所侵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　春，在知郓州任，有诗述怀。作品：淮南汶上三见春物有感。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一三。）</span><div id='poem_106920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮南汶上三见春物有感</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106920")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106920'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106920'>一麾南北数移官，三见莺花送雁寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106920'>双鬓欺人还似雪，寸心忧国本如丹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106920'>雕虫曲艺论文浅，乘障迂儒破敌难。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106920'>惟有归耕初志在，故田西接饮牛滩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106920'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年11月</a>　十一月，在知郓州任，以南郊礼，获进阶加恩，有谢表。作品：谢郊祀加恩表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢郊祀加恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155516")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155516'>礼天拜胙，甫毕于鸿仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155516_comment'></div>括土均休，汎沾于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155516_comment'></div>罔功内省，悸魄无从<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155516_comment'></div>窃念臣本以空疏，误承简拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155516_comment'></div>玷从官而积岁，尸荣禄以浮人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155516_comment'></div>凡最所更，风猷蔑树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155516_comment'></div>曲荷天私之覆，靡循官式之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155516_comment'></div>超践谏垣，预闻宰牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155516_comment'></div>属兵农之并讲，当朝夕之勤咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155516_comment'></div>徒竭陋愚，无裨纪律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155516_comment'></div>力穷犹驾，众知败驭之伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155516_comment'></div>物重过权，始验持衡之殆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155516_comment'></div>遭时宽政，勿汝深疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155516_comment'></div>假淮国之一麾，贸龙躔之再集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155516_comment'></div>皇心念旧，秘秩升华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155516_comment'></div>移守汶田，坐丰周粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155516_comment'></div>会于郊而陟配，嗟守土之恪居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155516_comment'></div>微藿翘诚，孤匏拥叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155516_comment'></div>敢谓伏蒙尊号皇帝陛下回舆作解，舍爵推慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155516_comment'></div>因劳臣工之勤，胥暨州藩之广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155516_comment'></div>纶书懋赏，星驿驰音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155516_comment'></div>衍多邑于旧封，倍荣租于真实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155516_comment'></div>命成难拒，恩溢无涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155516_comment'></div>矧笾豆骏奔，莫睹陪祀之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155516_comment'></div>而公卿奉引，了无承乏之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155516_comment'></div>逮流庆之丛臻，亦腼颜而虚受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155516_comment'></div>忍惭云极，度德奚堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155516_comment'></div>惟馀顶踵之微，或效涓埃之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155516_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1155516_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155516'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155516_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月29日</a>　正月二十九日，在知郓州任，复拜参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年2月</a>　二月，在知郓州任，上表乞罢参知政事。作品：再入参乞罢免重任表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再入参乞罢免重任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155534")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155534'>臣闻绠短而使汲渊，非浸灌之巧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155534_comment'></div>马穷而后易驾，非驰驭之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155534_comment'></div>物理苟然，人情可喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155534_comment'></div>是以明主临下，孤臣事君，弗强所能，乃辑宿官之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155534_comment'></div>自涯其分，方逃不职之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155534_comment'></div>敢傍斯言，用敷至恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155534_comment'></div>臣某<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃念臣天畀疏拙，地出羁单。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155534_comment'></div>偶缘挟册之勤，误中抡材之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155534_comment'></div>束绅仕路，佔毕文林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155534_comment'></div>遭山薮之兼容，备闺台之旅进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155534_comment'></div>自尔朝多过听，官匪序迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155534_comment'></div>骤尘星掖之华，深入銮坡之秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155534_comment'></div>固无寸效，可称明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155534_comment'></div>更因承乏之辰，猥玷参机之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155534_comment'></div>前叨未补，来忝益滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155534_comment'></div>过中之器易盈，责实之名难副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155534_comment'></div>果烦罢免，终赐保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155534_comment'></div>历典州符，五新年籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155534_comment'></div>何意君环之召，复联公衮之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155534_comment'></div>颠蘖再条，朽肌还肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155534_comment'></div>虽闻弦戢翼，悸魄未安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155534_comment'></div>而内手扪心，丹诚故在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155534_comment'></div>辄复夜思昼过，今计昨非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155534_comment'></div>期一得于陋愚，或少裨于顾访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155534_comment'></div>其如性资有限，机务至丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155534_comment'></div>卜式朴忠，初无趣和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155534_comment'></div>倪宽懦武，□□□明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155534_comment'></div>而又睿德日跻，圣猷天建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155534_comment'></div>按循先烈，裁定懿纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155534_comment'></div>求百辟之谠言，责三公之吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155534_comment'></div>谅非隽辅，畴克同寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155534_comment'></div>窃顾妄庸，将焉报称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155534_comment'></div>宜从重劾，以警空餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155534_comment'></div>然念竭智以进思，介一心而自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1155534_comment'></div>偶逃多悔，幸及三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1155534_comment'></div>稽大比之文，敢烦陟状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1155534_comment'></div>抚不肖之质，尤合避贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1155534_comment'></div>辄循考绩之期，仰丐退身之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1155534_comment'></div>伏望体天法道钦文聪武圣神孝德皇帝陛下廓包荒之度，推养士之慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1155534_comment'></div>业已与成，则无令亟败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1155534_comment'></div>事容善始，则当俾有终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1155534_comment'></div>许辞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1155534", 1155534, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>贰政</span>之繁，却服从臣之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1155534_comment'></div>职劳有底，量力自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1155534_comment'></div>亦冀穆穆公言，潜弭旷官之诮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1155534_comment'></div>谆谆末路，免罹不衷之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1155534_comment'></div>意迫言芜，期于得请，干冒宸扆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1155534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155534'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷四一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155534_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年2月</a>　二月，在知郓州任，有诗答弟宋祁，表白归隐之心。作品：答子京。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_106943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答子京</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106943")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106943'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106943'>一辞云陛五周年，琐闼销符宠再迁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106943'>时誉敢希吴陆俊，归心偏识汉疏贤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106943'>蜗头狼籍争锋地，鸿影徘徊避弋天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106943'>命驾不须频见约，颍滨嵩麓有私田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106943'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106943_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
洛阳

id='poem_sentence_0_107094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107094'>往非堪咋舌，来宠梦惊魂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107094'>病与疑弓释，身随散栎存。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107094'>惟馀太阳照，终不碍孤盆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107094'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_107094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_107094'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_107094_0'>⑴ 自注：余罢相蒙恩改官加职，非待罪之本望。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_107094_0'>⑵ 自注：至洛踰月，凡两蒙遣使传宣复问。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_107094_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　夏，在知河南府任，仁宗两次遣使存问，有谢表。作品：谢赐抚问表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐抚问表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155531")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155531_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155531'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155531'>使驲驰星，天辞出綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155531_comment'></div>辱宸心之念旧，因颁式以推慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155531_comment'></div>恩厚忘言，感深成泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155531_comment'></div>臣某诚荣诚感，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155531_comment'></div>窃念臣本由寒士，早玷荣班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155531_comment'></div>出入近司，周旋二纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155531_comment'></div>石心许国，固无可转之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155531_comment'></div>川谤盈朝，容致他来之吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155531_comment'></div>逮违枢握，荐易侯藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155531_comment'></div>席槐府之崇联，惕将坛之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155531_comment'></div>敢谓皇帝陛下尧仁无外，汉度兼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155531_comment'></div>谓体貌之尝加，眷忠愚而可悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155531_comment'></div>爰驰华牡，俾道温言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155531_comment'></div>荈焙惟珍，特分于贡品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155531_comment'></div>宝奁有烂，纷照于私闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155531_comment'></div>仰聆金玉之音，俾极君臣之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155531_comment'></div>孤生内省，隆惠奚酬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155531_comment'></div>但归誓于糜捐，或谢生于覆育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155531_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1155531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155531'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三六。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155531_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　冬，在知河南府任，石扬休寄诗十首，依韵和之。作品：次韵和石学士见寄十首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_106408' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　约于本年，在知河南府任，辟宋敏求通判西京留守司。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　约于本年，在知河南府任，有诗自嘲。作品：时贤多以不才诮我因自咏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_106669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106669'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106669'>我本无心士，终非济世才。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年8月</a>　八月，在知河南府任，有诗和吴育。作品：次韵和新命留台吴侍郎自适之作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_106633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和新命留台吴侍郎自适之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106633")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106633'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106633'>谢病弥年叹偃床，知君灵气本无伤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106633'>论筌自识忘筌意，失马终为得马祥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
许昌（长社）

id='poem_sentence_2_106484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年闰3月</a>　闰三月，在知许州任，游西湖，有诗。作品：闰三月再到西湖，花卉已过，春余夏早，景物亦佳，因复留连，日夕忘返。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_106675' id='poem_title_106854_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_106854_0'>① 按：宋王楙《野客丛书》卷一九引《西清诗话》云：许昌西湖展江亭就，宋元宪留题。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106854'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106854'>绿鸭东陂已可怜，更因云窦注西田。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106854'>凿开鱼鸟忘情地，展尽江河极目天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106854'>向夕旧滩都浸月，过寒新树便留烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106854'>使君直欲称渔叟，愿赐閒州不计年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106854'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106854_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_106853' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106853' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106853?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106853_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106853'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106853'>西北云波逗异津，两陂相合到城闉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106853'>桥横断岸才通舫，路转新洲不踏尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106853'>倒影剩容霞底日，暖光平展鉴中春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106853'>摧颓病守时无用，堪与鸥鹇作主人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106853_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106853'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106853_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年5月3日</a>　五月三日，在知许州任，以兵部尚书徙知河阳。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
孟州（河阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ca1a1a736ade43e6873d7f725dc751f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ca1a1a736ade43e6873d7f725dc751f9");'><span id='ca1a1a736ade43e6873d7f725dc751f9_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年7月</a>　七月，到知河阳任，有谢表。作品：河阳谢到任表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>河阳谢到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155523")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155523'>进联省坐，易抚侯封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155523_comment'></div>促驾启行，适临治所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155523_comment'></div>选辰署事，初布藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155523_comment'></div>祗荷奖甄，不胜荣惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155523_comment'></div>臣某诚感诚抃，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155523_comment'></div>窃念臣一蒙策免，三宠州迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155523_comment'></div>禄有空餐，官无最状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155523_comment'></div>向属盟津之缺守，猥烦汉札之疏恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155523_comment'></div>升秩夏卿，增华使棨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155523_comment'></div>仍因便道，特许过都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155523_comment'></div>朝推念旧之慈，礼借仪台之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155523_comment'></div>孤心易感，危涕难收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155523_comment'></div>寻迫王程，遽开郡阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155523_comment'></div>此州据山河之会，拥周、晋之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155523_comment'></div>列戍分城，造舟济险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155523_comment'></div>堤防甚设，讥逻为严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155523_comment'></div>虽曰近藩，实名雄镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155523_comment'></div>然而累年饥旱，比日沈灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155523_comment'></div>东有漕渠开塞之烦，北有计檄诛求之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155523_comment'></div>使多缘隙，民罕聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155523_comment'></div>臣敢不略去烦苛，勤加绥辑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155523_comment'></div>庶臻还定，少副忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155523_comment'></div>俯循备御之馀，曷称惟良之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155523_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下俯矜忠朴，本乏同游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155523_comment'></div>因寰服之奥区，进天台之峻品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155523_comment'></div>曲加存遇，终保衰迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155523_comment'></div>身远天高，恩深语拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155523_comment'></div>惟有涕泗，尚冀感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155523_comment'></div>臣无任戴天荷圣激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1155523_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155523'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155523_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　本年，在知河阳任，有诗和庞籍。作品：淳之太尉相公寄示赴镇小编，三复成诵，研味之余，理当酬继，但难于遍和，辄取首题，赋成拙句一首，既伸高山仰止之愿，并以为谢。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_title_1155533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155533'>宫闱延庆，国邑疏封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155533_comment'></div>诞告有初，均欢无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155533_comment'></div>臣某诚欣诚抃，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155533_comment'></div>伏以兖国公主天孙禀粹，巽女流占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155533_comment'></div>在姆不勤，承亲允穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155533_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下至仁敷祐，笃爱成雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155533_comment'></div>诞生秾矣之姿，前导百斯之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155533_comment'></div>教宫有典，择配惟嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155533_comment'></div>爰选良辰，茂宣华册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155533_comment'></div>肇禹州而启国，筑鲁馆以由章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155533_comment'></div>典物备臻，官司载跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155533_comment'></div>矧于归夫舅族，谅深沐于皇慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155533_comment'></div>臣早忝近班，今司外服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155533_comment'></div>徒聆发号，莫获观光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155533_comment'></div>瞻望宸廷，臣无任。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年6月</a>　六月，在知河阳任，有谢表。作品：谢诏赴阙表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢诏赴阙表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1155521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155521'>使驲光华，甫临州部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155521_comment'></div>言纶温密，申锡诏函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155521_comment'></div>闻命震惶，抚躬跼蹐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155521_comment'></div>臣某诚荣诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155521_comment'></div>窃念臣向辞宰政，出布藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155521_comment'></div>专处外以首公，顾还朝而绝望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155521_comment'></div>周旋三任，首尾八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155521_comment'></div>终微树化之方，可称惟良之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155521_comment'></div>比者伏蒙皇帝陛下追怜旧物，均赋群材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155521_comment'></div>谕发号之扬庭，俾解藩而趋节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155521_comment'></div>孤臣何幸，丕训前颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155521_comment'></div>未知让爵之端，先耸捐生之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155521_comment'></div>感深成泣，言拙无文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155521_comment'></div>方促驾以就途，但望云而翘首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155521_comment'></div>永言归报，倍万常钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155521_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1155521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155521'><span id='poem_title_107157' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/107157?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄子京<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span "poem_title_107157")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_107157_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_107157_0'>① 为郡八年，荣愿已息，朝恩念旧，复假相印管内枢，然思归之心日以忉怛矣</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_107157'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_107157'>八年三郡驾朱轮，更忝鸿枢对国均。<div id='poem_sentence_0_107157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_107157'>老去师丹多忘事，少来之武不如人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_107157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_107157'>车中顾马空能数，海上逢鸥想见亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_107157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_107157'>惟有弟兄归隐志，共将耕凿报尧仁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_107157_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_107157'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_107157_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
安阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0aaa333381a6422c8168816cf5c33ced_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0aaa333381a6422c8168816cf5c33ced");'><span id='0aaa333381a6422c8168816cf5c33ced_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1062')">1061-1062年</a>，66-67岁</div><div id='0aaa333381a6422c8168816cf5c33ced' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　本年，徙知相州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　春，在知相州任，有诗述怀。作品：相州春日。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_106778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>相州春日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106778")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106778'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106778'>北土无繁卉，空亭有暝阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106778'>狂飞憎野絮，多舌恨春禽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106778'>地燥山如朽，池寒水不深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106778'>生平箕颍志，轩冕独何心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　本年，在知相州任，上表乞致仕。作品：乞致仕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　本年，在知相州任，再上表乞致仕，被召还。作品：乞致仕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
亳州（谯县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf04f99199b94bf2a87a4727b404c190_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf04f99199b94bf2a87a4727b404c190");'><span id='bf04f99199b94bf2a87a4727b404c190_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>，69岁</div><div id='bf04f99199b94bf2a87a4727b404c190' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年6月14日</a>　六月十四日，在知亳州任，诏大敕系位在皇子赵颢之前。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　本年，在知亳州任，又上表请老，以司空致仕。作品：再乞致仕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《元宪集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1155537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1155537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1155537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_1155537")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1155537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1155537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1155537'>笔端言拙，悃愊难敷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1155537_comment'></div>诏底恩隆，都俞尚閟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1155537_comment'></div>辄缘洪造，更露微衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1155537_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1155537_comment'></div>伏念臣草茅地寒，樗栎材散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1155537_comment'></div>曩因薄技，来会亨辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1155537_comment'></div>列仕版者再闰八周，佐国论者五迁三已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1155537_comment'></div>每尘眷奖，遂极崇高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1155537_comment'></div>风绩蔑升，年华滋晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1155537_comment'></div>顷希止足，姑解组于邺城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1155537_comment'></div>比恤蹒跚，复假麾于谯壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1155537_comment'></div>腼颜冒禄，力疾长人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1155537_comment'></div>惟知谨守常规，郡阁靡颁条之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1155537_comment'></div>不能导迎善气，农畴罹洚水之灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1155537_comment'></div>加以淮北荒残，涡阳沮洳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1155537_comment'></div>萧然南亩，悉变于横流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1155537_comment'></div>蕞尔孤城，不沈者数版。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1155537_comment'></div>眷言守土，尤藉长才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1155537_comment'></div>而臣适在暮龄，猥当优寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1155537_comment'></div>敢卧尸于重禄，空勉率于孱躯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1155537_comment'></div>因此震惊，转成羸薾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1155537_comment'></div>而况任崇将钺，秩视公槐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1155537_comment'></div>固当参宠勋贤，讵可久私癃瘵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1155537_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下大明委照，广覆推慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1155537_comment'></div>矜齿发之早衰，悯筋骸之难强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1155537_comment'></div>俾从閒秩，允谓生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1155537_comment'></div>矧在先朝，已陈纳禄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1155537_comment'></div>连逢圣日，遽此延恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1155537_comment'></div>出入三年，倦勤十上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1155537_comment'></div>昔祈退老，固沥恳于朝端；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1155537_comment'></div>今若因循，必取嗤于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1155537_comment'></div>非独失臣子进退之节，抑亦玷衣冠廉让之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1155537_comment'></div>倾藿驰诚，叫阍伫可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1155537_comment'></div>伏乞检会前奏，特除臣一致仕官，放归田里。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1155537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1155537'><span class='label'>按：</span>《宋元宪集》卷一九。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷四一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1155537_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　本年，乘船自亳州返汴京，有诗。作品：致仕得请泛舟归第。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《元宪集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_106876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_106876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/106876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>致仕得请泛舟归第</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(24786, "北宋", "宋庠", "poem_title_106876")'>宋庠</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_106876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_106876'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_106876'>辅郡初辞节，孤舟始去官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_106876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_106876'>桥头帆影急，枕底浪声寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_106876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_106876'>好爵云谁宠，危心且自安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_106876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_106876'>赐车诚可爱，閒共子孙看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_106876_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_106876'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_106876_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
